# Detection and Divination

Use these for sensing, knowledge gathering, revelation, and information access. Covers scrying, detection, and knowledge-access powers.

<div class="power-card" markdown="1">

## Detect Evil

> **Detect Evil**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 2 **R:** self  
> **T:** hostile intent signatures within short range (~18 m / 60 ft) **D:** 2 turns (~20 minutes)
>
> You scan for active malign intent, predatory will, or hostile enchanted influence in nearby creatures and objects. This reads threat-leaning resonance rather than strict cosmic alignment labels.
>
> Ambiguous entities may register as faint or unstable signals.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - distinguish immediate hostile intent from latent danger; x4 - briefly mark strongest detected source with a visible omen-glow.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [divination]
>   [detection]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Basic Rules; spell: Detect Evil
>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: Detect Evil
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Detect Evil
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Detect Evil; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Detect Evil
> Range: 120'
> Duration: 2 turns
> Effect: Reveals evil intent or influence
>
> This spell detects evil or hostile influence
> in nearby creatures, objects, or effects,
> depending on context and edition wording.

  <div class="power-return">

## Detect Magic

> **Detect Magic**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 2 **R:** self  
> **T:** all magical presences within short range (~18 m / 60 ft) **D:** 2 turns (~20 minutes)
>
> Your sight shifts into a diagnostic register. Magical objects, creatures, fields, and places within range glow with visible signature-light. This is a detection and triage tool rather than a full analysis engine: it reveals presence, not complete function.
>
> Hidden magic behind solid containers, sealed walls, or similar barriers may remain concealed even when the ambient field is visible nearby.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — distinguish active effects from dormant enchantments; x4 — isolate the strongest magical source in range even if lesser glows overlap.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [divination]
>   [detection]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Basic Rules; spell: Detect Magic
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Detect Magic
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Detect Magic; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Detect Magic
> Range: 0
> Duration: 2 turns
> Effect: Everything within 60'
>
> When this spell is cast, the magic-user
> will see all magical objects, creatures,
> and places within range glow. This effect
> will not last very long, and should be
> saved until the magic-user wants to see if
> something found during an adventure
> is, in fact, magical. Example: Shortly
> after casting this spell, a magic-user
> walks into a room containing a door
> locked by magic, a magical potion laying
> nearby, and a treasure chest containing a
> magic wand. All the magic will glow, but
> only the door and potion will be seen;
> the light of the glowing wand is hidden
> by the treasure chest.

  <div class="power-return">
    &nbsp;&nbsp;
    <a class="js-back-link" href="#chapter-06-power-index-anchor" aria-label="Back to previous page">
      ↩ Back
    </a>
  </div>

</div>

<div class="power-card" markdown="1">

## Infravision

> **Infravision**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 6 **R:** touch  
> **T:** one living creature **D:** 1 day
>
> The target gains heat-sensing vision out to 18 m (60 ft) in complete darkness. Warm creatures and objects appear in red tones; cold items and terrain register as blue or dark. Fine detail sufficient for combat, navigation, and reading body positions is available — but not fine enough to read text. Bright light can dazzle infravision just as it can dazzle normal sight.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — extend range to 36 m, or grant infravision to all touched targets simultaneously (up to your Level); x4 — grant full thermic-imaging sight to see temperature gradients through thin barriers (cloth, wood, light wall sections) as well as open space.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:fantascience]
>   [storage:item]
>   [sensory]
>   [enhancement]
>   [darkness]
>   [utility]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: Infravision
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Infravision
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Infravision; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Infravision
> Range: Touch
> Duration: 1 day
> Effect: One living creature
>
> This spell enables the recipient to see in
> the dark, to a 60' range. Warm things
> appear red, cold things appear blue or
> black. Fine detail (sufficient for combat
> and navigation) is possible but not fine
> enough to read by. Bright light or a light
> spell can temporarily dazzle infravision.

  <div class="power-return">
    &nbsp;&nbsp;
    <a class="js-back-link" href="#chapter-06-power-index-anchor" aria-label="Back to previous page">
      ↩ Back
    </a>

## Detect Invisible

> **Detect Invisible**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 4 **R:** self  
> **T:** unseen entities and fields within short range (~18 m / 60 ft) **D:** 6 turns (~1 hour)
>
> Your perception shifts into an anti-concealment register. Invisible creatures, hidden magical surfaces, and otherwise unseen entities within range become visible as distortion outlines or luminous traces.
>
> This does not automatically reveal full identity, alignment, or intent; it reveals presence and approximate location.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — maintain clear detection through light cover and smoke; x4 — also reveal recently traversed invisible movement trails from the last minute.
>
> See also: `Eyes of Akaula` in the SDM Powers Index for a broader reveal/divination variant.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [divination]
>   [detection]
>   [anti-concealment]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: Detect Invisible
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Detect Invisible
>   - file: Synthetic_Dream_Machine_04_Powers_Index.md; related: Eyes of Akaula
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Detect Invisible; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Detect Invisible
> Range: 0
> Duration: 6 turns
> Effect: Everything within 10'
>
> This spell allows the caster to see all
> invisible creatures and objects within range
> for the duration. It reveals hidden presence,
> but not full magical analysis.

## ESP

> **ESP**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 4 **R:** self  
> **T:** intelligent minds within medium range (~18 m / 60 ft, barrier-limited) **D:** 12 turns (~2 hours)
>
> You open a constrained thought-sense channel that surfaces nearby conscious mental activity as impressions, emotional spikes, and fragmentary intent. It is strongest on uncloaked, nonshielded minds.
>
> Dense metal barriers, lead sheathing, and dedicated anti-divination effects can block the channel.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - isolate one target mind for clearer thematic reads; x4 - detect concealed observers through thin barriers via thought-echo bleed.
>
> See also: `Yellow Foresight` in the SDM Powers Index for a broad sentience-scan cousin.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [divination]
>   [mental]
>   [detection]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: ESP
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: ESP
>   - file: Synthetic_Dream_Machine_04_Powers_Index.md; related: Yellow Foresight
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: ESP; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> ESP
> Range: 60'
> Duration: 12 turns
> Effect: Reads surface thoughts
>
> This spell allows the caster to detect or
> read nearby thoughts, usually constrained
> by shielding materials and distance.

  <div class="power-return">
    &nbsp;&nbsp;
    <a class="js-back-link" href="#chapter-06-power-index-anchor" aria-label="Back to previous page">
      ↩ Back
    </a>
  </div>

<div class="power-card" markdown="1">

## Clairvoyance

> **Clairvoyance**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 6 **R:** far (~20 m / 60 ft from chosen anchor)  
> **T:** one remote visual point **D:** 12 turns
>
> You establish a floating sight-sensor at a chosen location within range and perceive from that vantage as if your eye were physically present there. The sensor remains fixed unless the referee permits subtle drift.
>
> This provides sight only; sound and full multispectral readouts require additional powers.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - also gain faint audio impressions near the sensor point; x4 - split attention between your body and sensor view without action penalty.
>
> See also: `Eyes of the Arrow` in the SDM Powers Index for a mobile projectile-bound remote sensor variant.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [divination]
>   [scrying]
>   [detection]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: Clairvoyance
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Clairvoyance
>   - file: Synthetic_Dream_Machine_04_Powers_Index.md; related: Eyes of the Arrow
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Clairvoyance; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Clairvoyance
> Range: 60'
> Duration: 12 turns
> Effect: One remote view point
>
> This spell lets the caster see through a
> distant point in space, enabling remote
> visual reconnaissance and scene awareness.

## Wizard Eye

> **Wizard Eye**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 8 **R:** far (~72 m / 240 ft leash)  
> **T:** one mobile arcane eye-sensor **D:** 6 turns
>
> You project a moving observation orb that you can steer through corridors, chambers, and exposed approaches. You see through the eye as it travels, making it ideal for scouting trapped routes and blind corners without exposing your body.
>
> The eye moves deliberately and can be blocked by solid barriers and anti-divination wards.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - increase travel leash and movement speed; x4 - eye relays crude spectral highlights (heat, life-sign motion, active magic glow).

## Locate Object

> **Locate Object**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 4 **R:** self  
> **T:** one named or clearly-described object type **D:** 2 turns (~20 minutes)
>
> You establish a directional lock on a specific object, or on the nearest object matching a precise category description. While active, you always know relative bearing and broad distance trend (closer/farther) as long as the target remains within effective search radius.
>
> Strong anti-divination wards, noosphere-jamming architecture, or deep lead-lined barriers may block the lock.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — broaden to up to three specific object signatures; x4 — maintain lock while moving quickly and through one major obstruction boundary.

## Read Magic

> **Read Magic**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 2 **R:** self  
> **T:** one magical inscription, glyph sequence, codex page, or scroll **D:** 2 turns (~20 minutes)
>
> You align your perception with encoded arcana syntax and can decipher magical writing normally unreadable to unaided sight. This enables safe interpretation of scrolls, formulae, and ward-script under calm conditions.
>
> This does not cast the decoded effect by itself; it grants intelligible access.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - decode one additional linked text in the same scene; x4 - retain stable recall of decoded structure until next dawn.

> Spoken fluency is not guaranteed; this is reading bridge first.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - maintain comprehension while transcribing at speed; x4 - temporary spoken bridge for one short exchange in the same language family.

## Find Traps

> **Find Traps**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 4 **R:** self  
> **T:** all trap signatures within 9 m / 30 ft **D:** 2 turns (~20 minutes)
>
> You tune your perception to hostile trigger geometry. Traps within 30 feet register as a dull blue noospheric glow, allowing rapid hazard mapping while moving through unknown interiors.
>
> The power reveals presence, not mechanism: it does not identify exact trigger type, bypass method, or disarm sequence.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — extend scan radius to 18 m / 60 ft; x4 — each revealed trap also gives one brief clue about likely trigger medium (pressure, line, arcane ward, etc.).

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]

>   [detection]
>   [utility]

osr:
> Find Traps
> Range: 0 (Cleric only)
> Duration: 2 turns
> Effect: Traps within 30' glow
>
> This spell causes all traps to glow with a
> dull blue light when the cleric comes
> within 30' of them. It does not reveal the
> trap type, nor methods of removing it.

## Know Alignment

> **Know Alignment**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 4 **R:** self (target within touch range)  
> **T:** one creature, item, or small area **D:** 1 round
>
> You read ethical-vector resonance and reveal whether a target trends Lawful, Neutral, or Chaotic. This also works on enchanted objects or consecrated/profaned spaces where alignment imprinting is present.
>
> _Reversible — Confuse Alignment:_ By touch, you scramble one target's alignment signature for 1 turn per user Level. During this time, alignment-reading effects return a consistent but false result. No save.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — also detect whether the reading is naturally anchored or externally imposed; x4 — reveal one recent shift in the target's alignment trend if the referee judges evidence exists.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [divination]
>   [alignment]
>   [reversible]
>   [cleric]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: Know Alignment
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Know Alignment
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Know Alignment; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Know Alignment*
> Range: 0 (Cleric only)
> Duration: 1 round
> Effect: One creature within 10'
>
> The caster discovers the alignment of one
> nearby creature (or an enchanted item or
> area). The reverse, confuse alignment,
> lasts 1 turn per caster level, is cast by
> touch with no Save, and causes future
> alignment checks to return a false answer.

## Speak with Animals

> **Speak with Animals**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 4 **R:** self  
> **T:** one named animal type within 9 m / 30 ft **D:** 6 turns (~1 hour)
>
> You establish a temporary language bridge with one specific kind of normal or giant animal. For the duration, creatures of that type within range can understand you, and you can understand them in return. Their reactions skew favorable, and simple favors may be negotiated if the request is within their natural ability.
>
> This does not affect intelligent beast-folk or fantastic creatures.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — maintain the bridge with two related animal types; x4 — also gain a brief sensory impression of the local territory from the animals you question.

>   [power]

> Speak with Animals
> Range: 0 (Cleric only)
> Duration: 6 turns
> Effect: Allows conversation within 30'
>
> The cleric names one animal type and may
> then speak with all animals of that type
> within 30'. Reactions are usually favorable,
> and a possible favor may be negotiated if
> the animal can understand and perform it.

## Speak with the Dead

> **Speak with the Dead**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 6 **R:** near (~3 m / 10 ft)  
> **T:** one corpse and the spirit linked to it **D:** 1 round per user Level
>
> You open a brief conversational channel to a deceased spirit through its body. During the effect you may ask up to 3 questions. The dead can answer only from knowledge held before death, and their clarity depends partly on how compatible their alignment was with yours.
>
> Low-level users can only reach the recently dead; greater mastery extends the reachable age of the spirit dramatically.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — ask one additional question; x4 — compel one answer to be unusually direct rather than evasive or symbolic.
>
> See also: `Speak With Husk` for a close SDM-facing corpse-conversation cousin.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [divination]
>   [communication]
>   [death]
>   [cleric]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: Speak with the Dead
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Speak with the Dead
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Speak with the Dead; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Speak with the Dead
> Range: 10'
> Duration: 1 round per level of the cleric
> Effect: Cleric may ask 3 questions
>
> The cleric may ask 3 questions of a
> deceased spirit if the body is within range.
> The spirit replies in a tongue known to the
> cleric, but only with knowledge up to the
> moment of death. Friendly alignment gives
> clearer answers; differing alignment may
> produce riddling replies.

  <div class="power-return">

## Find the Path

> **Find the Path**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 12 **R:** self  
> **T:** one specifically named destination **D:** 6 turns + 1 turn per user Level
>
> You lock onto a named destination and receive route-certainty guidance: heading direction, hidden entry hints, and key passage constraints needed to reach it.
>
> While active, this power can surface operational wayfinding details such as concealed doors, required passwords, or local traversal constraints.
>
> The moment you attempt to write down, record, or disclose those special details, the special insight collapses and only general direction remains.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — include one allied navigator in the guidance field; x4 — suppress one local path-obfuscation effect for the duration.

> Range: 0 (Cleric only)
> Duration: 6 turns + 1 turn per level
> Effect: Shows path to an area
>
> The caster names a specific place and
> knows direction plus special routing
> information (secret doors, passwords,
> and similar) needed to reach it.

## Truesight

> **Truesight**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 10 **R:** self  
> **T:** all phenomena within ~36 m / 120 ft **D:** 1 turn + 1 round per user Level
>
> You perceive underlying reality through concealment layers. Hidden, invisible, ethereal, disguised, polymorphed, and otherwise masked entities appear in true form.
>
> Secret doors and deception overlays become legible. Alignment and practical power tier also register as clear noospheric signatures.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — extend range to 180 ft; x4 — mark one seen deception source with a visible reveal-sigil allies can follow for one scene.

## Speak with Monsters

> **Speak with Monsters**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 12 **R:** self (conversation within ~9 m / 30 ft)  
> **T:** living and undead creatures in range **D:** 1 round per user Level
>
> You establish a temporary universal negotiation channel with monsters in range, including unintelligent and undead beings. While active, targets can understand and answer questions.
>
> Creatures engaged in conversation do not attack you unless attacked first, though they may defend themselves or flee. You may ask one question per round.
>
> _Reverse — Babble:_ Target one creature within 60 ft; on failed Save vs. Spells (with -2 penalty), all communication attempts by the target become unusable noise for 1 turn per user Level.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — allow one nearby ally to share the channel; x4 — each answered question may include one brief clarifying follow-up.
>
> See also: `Anti-Babylon` as a broad SDM language-bridge cousin.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]

>   [communication]
>   [reversible]
>   [high-tier]

> Range: 0 (Cleric only)
> Duration: 1 round per level
> Effect: Conversation with any monster
>
> Allows the cleric to converse with living
> and undead monsters within 30'. One
> question may be asked per round. Reverse
> form (Babble) disrupts one target's ability
> to communicate.

## Commune

> **Commune**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 10 **R:** self  
> **T:** one higher-power consultation channel **D:** up to 3 turns
>
> You open a constrained consultation link with a greater intelligence aligned to your doctrine, shrine-lineage, or cosmic sponsor. During the active window, you may ask up to three yes/no questions and receive clear binary responses.
>
> The channel has strict cadence limits. Standard use is once per week; frequent overuse can trigger silence, static, symbolic noise, or referee-imposed petition delays.
>
> Annual observance clause: on a major holy day or equivalent anchor date, question capacity may double at referee discretion.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - permit one allied officiant to co-witness one answer; x4 - one answer may be expanded from binary to a short caution phrase.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [divination]
>   [oracle]
>   [ritual]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Companion Set; spell: Commune
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Commune
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Commune; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Commune
> Range: 0 (Cleric only)
> Duration: 3 turns
> Effect: 3 questions
>
> The cleric may ask three yes/no questions
> of greater powers. Use is normally limited
> to once per week, with occasional special
> observance exceptions allowing more.

  <div class="power-return">
    &nbsp;&nbsp;

## Faerie Fire

> **Faerie Fire**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 2 **R:** near (~18 m / 60 ft)  
> **T:** one or more detected creatures/objects outlined by up to 12 ft of glow per 5 user Levels **D:** 1 round per user Level
>
> You outline targets in pale flickering green fire that causes no direct damage but makes them conspicuous and easier to strike.
>
> Attacks against outlined targets gain +2 to hit. Targets can be selected if detected by any valid means (sight, detect effects, tracking cues, and similar).
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - intensify outline so invisible targets lose most concealment benefits; x4 - marked targets also suffer disadvantage on stealth checks while the effect lasts.

tags:
>   [power]

> Range: 60'
> Duration: 1 round per level of caster
> Effect: Illuminates creatures or objects
>
> Outlines targets in harmless green fire.
> Attacks against outlined targets gain +2.
> The caster can outline more total size at
> higher levels.

## Predict Weather

> **Predict Weather**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 2 **R:** self  
> **T:** regional weather forecast field (1 mile diameter per user Level) **D:** 12 hours of forecast knowledge
>
> You receive an accurate forecast of coming weather over a broad region keyed to your current location.
>
> This grants prediction only, not control. Use it for route planning, hazard prep, and timing-sensitive operations.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - include trend confidence on severe shifts (storms, sudden wind turns, heavy temperature drops); x4 - gain one pinpoint timing window for a selected weather threshold event.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [divination]
>   [weather]
>   [druid]

meta:

>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Predict Weather
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Predict Weather
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Predict Weather; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Predict Weather
> Range: 0 (druid only)
> Duration: 12 hours
> Effect: Gives knowledge of coming weather
>
> Reveals accurate weather for the next
> 12 hours across 1 mile diameter per level
> of the caster. Provides information only.

  <div class="power-return">
    &nbsp;&nbsp;
    <a class="js-back-link" href="#chapter-06-power-index-anchor" aria-label="Back to previous page">

## Detect Danger

> **Detect Danger**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 2 **R:** near scan radius (5 ft / 1.5 m per user Level)  
> **T:** one examined creature/object/zone at a time **D:** 1 hour (or 3 turns outside natural prime conditions)
>
> You assess nearby entities for immediate, potential, or benign threat posture from your current perspective. Includes poison detection and trap-like hazard awareness cues.
>
> Requires focused examination cadence: roughly one round per small object/creature or one square-foot zone.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - classify one additional likely hazard vector (poison, collapse, ambush trigger, or volatile aura) with each scan; x4 - briefly expose one hidden danger signature as a visible omen mark for allies.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [divination]
>   [hazard]
>   [druid]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Detect Danger
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Detect Danger
>   - file: Synthetic_Dream_Machine_04_Powers_Index.md; related: Yellow Foresight
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Detect Danger; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Detect Danger
> Range: 5' per level of the caster
> Duration: One hour
> Effect: Reveals hazards
>
> Combines hazard and threat sensing,
> classifying examined targets as immediate,
> potential, or benign dangers and detecting
> poisons other scans might miss.

## Analyze

> **Analyze**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 2 **R:** touch  
> **T:** one magical item **D:** 1 round
>
> You handle a magical item — holding, wearing, or placing it as required — and attempt to read its enchantment. The identification chance is 15% plus 5% per user Level.
>
> Results are deliberately vague: a weapon's bonus registers as "many" or "few" rather than a precise number; charge counts read within ±25% of the true total; type and purpose give a rough impression rather than a name. Non-magical items are identified as such on a success.
>
> **Caution:** Any consequences of handling the item (curses, booby-traps, activation conditions) fall on the user at the moment of contact. Normal saving throws apply.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — identify two magical properties in the same round; x4 — suppresses any activation or curse trigger for the duration of the reading only.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [divination]
>   [identification]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Analyze
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Analyze; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Analyze
> Range: Touch
> Duration: 1 round
> Effect: Analyzes magic on one item
>
> 15% + 5%/level chance per property. Must physically hold/wear the
> item (curse/trap consequences still apply). Results are vague.
> Non-magical items identified as such. RC-only provenance.

  <div class="power-return">
    &nbsp;&nbsp;
    <a class="js-back-link" href="#chapter-06-power-index-anchor" aria-label="Back to previous page">
      ↩ Back
    </a>
  </div>

## Speak with Plants

> **Speak with Plants**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 8 **R:** self (plants within ~9 m / 30 ft)  
> **T:** all plants and plant-like creatures within 30 ft **D:** 3 turns
>
> You open a channel of mutual intelligibility with plant life. For the duration you may speak with and understand any plant within range as if it were a willing conversationalist. Any reasonable favor within a plant's power — open a path through dense growth, describe who passed, lean aside — will be granted.
>
> This power also reaches plant-like monsters such as treants, allowing dialogue where combat might otherwise be the only option.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — extend range to 60 ft and include dormant or dead wood; x4 — request one active service from a plant that lasts beyond the spell duration until the task is complete or clearly impossible.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [divination]
>   [communication]
>   [plant]
>   [cleric]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: Speak with Plants
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Speak with Plants
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Speak with Plants; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Speak with Plants
> Range: 0 (cleric only)
> Duration: 3 turns
> Effect: All plants within 30'
>
> Two-way communication with plant life within 30'. Plants grant simple
> favors. Allows passage through impenetrable undergrowth. Includes
> plantlike monsters (treants). Source: Expert Set + RC.

  <div class="power-return">

## Contact Outer Plane

> **Contact Outer Plane**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 10 **R:** self
> **T:** one chosen outer-plane intelligence (Immortal-level) **D:** special (question window)
>
> You open directed mental contact with an outer-plane intelligence and ask a number of questions based on plane-distance. Farther planes permit more questions and better odds of useful answers, but sharply increase insanity risk.
>
> On activation, resolve insanity chance once for the chosen distance. If contact succeeds, each question may still yield truth, ignorance, or deception at referee call.
>
> Casting limit: at most once per month per user (or less often by referee doctrine). If insanity occurs, recovery requires weeks of rest equal to contacted-plane distance.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - ask one extra constrained question after the normal limit. x4 - reduce one step of answer ambiguity (lie -> unknown or unknown -> probable truth) for a single question, but always trigger a Dangerous Magic roll.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [divination]
>   [dangerous]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Companion Set; spell: Contact Outer Plane
>   - becmi:Immortals Set; spell: Contact Outer Plane
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Contact Outer Plane
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Contact Outer Plane; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Contact Outer Plane
> Range: 0 (spellcaster only)
> Duration: see below
> Effect: 3-12 questions may be answered
>
> Contacting a distant outer plane gives more questions and better knowledge odds, but increases insanity risk.
> Caster can use the spell once per month at most. Insanity recovery takes weeks equal to plane-distance.

</div>

## Lore

> **Lore**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 14 **R:** self
> **T:** one item, place, or person **D:** permanent insight after study interval
>
> You perform deep noospheric inquiry to extract hidden knowledge. Study time varies by target familiarity and distance: held items resolve quickly, remote or legendary subjects may require extended research windows.
>
> For held items, you can recover operational identity: name, command words, primary function, and approximate remaining charges.
>
> Multi-function artifacts may reveal only one function per casting.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - reduce research time tier by one bracket. x4 - gain one additional confirmed function or one clarified riddle-fragment.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [divination]
>   [research]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Lore
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Lore
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Lore; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Lore
> Range: 0 (magic-user only)
> Duration: Permanent
> Effect: Reveals details of 1 item, place, or person
>
> Held items resolve in 1d4 turns; remote or legendary targets may take up to 1d100 days.
> A single casting may reveal only one function of a multi-function item.

# Transformation and Alteration

Use these for shape-changing, transmutation, size modification, and material alteration. Covers polymorphic and transmutative effects.

<div class="power-card" markdown="1">

## Polymorph Self

> **Polymorph Self**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 8 **R:** self  
> **T:** self **D:** 6 turns + 1 turn per user Level
>
> You reconfigure your body into the physical form of another living creature whose Level does not exceed your own. You keep your own Life, saves, attack competence, and core durability, but gain the new form's physical movement and bodily capabilities. You do not gain supernatural immunities, breath weapons, spellcasting, or other special monster-side powers.
>
> While transformed, you cannot cast powers that require speech, gestures, or stable humanlike handling unless the referee judges the new form can actually perform them.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — shift once more into a different eligible form before the duration ends; x4 — retain simple speech and gear access if the chosen form plausibly supports both.
>
> See also: `Alter Self` and `Skinshift` in the SDM Powers Index for related self-transformation descendants.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [transformation]
>   [body]
>   [imbued]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: Polymorph Self
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Polymorph Self
>   - file: Synthetic_Dream_Machine_04_Powers_Index.md; related: Alter Self
>   - file: Synthetic_Dream_Machine_04_Powers_Index.md; related: Skinshift
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Polymorph Self; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Polymorph Self
> Range: 0 (Caster only)
> Duration: 6 turns + 1 turn per level of the
> caster
> Effect: Caster may change shapes
>
> This spell allows the caster to change
> shape, taking the physical form of another
> living creature. The Hit Dice of the new
> form must be equal to or less than the Hit
> Dice of the caster. The caster's Armor
> Class, hit points, Hit rolls, and Saving
> Throws do not change. Special abilities
> and special immunities of the new form
> are not gained, but physical abilities are ac-
> quired. For example, a magic-user poly-
> morphed into a frost giant has the strength
> of a frost giant and the ability to hurl boul-
> ders, but not immunity from cold. A
> magic-user polymorphed into a dragon
> could fly but would not be able to use any
> breath weapons or spells.
>
> Spells cannot be cast while polymorphed
> into a different form. The spell lasts for the
> given duration, or until dispelled, or until
> the caster is killed.

  <div class="power-return">
    &nbsp;&nbsp;
    <a class="js-back-link" href="#chapter-06-power-index-anchor" aria-label="Back to previous page">
      ↩ Back
    </a>

## Word of Recall

> **Word of Recall**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 12 **R:** self  
> **T:** caster plus carried equipment **D:** instant
>
> You trigger immediate return to your anchored sanctuary location (a prepared home meditation chamber). This is a one-caster extraction effect, not a group teleport.
>
> On the casting round, you automatically seize initiative unless surprised.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — include one bonded willing companion in contact; x4 — leave a fleeting return-trace for one round that can be followed only by specifically attuned allies.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [movement]
>   [teleport]
>   [sanctuary]
>   [high-tier]

>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Word of Recall
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Word of Recall; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Word of Recall
> Range: 0 (Cleric only)
> Duration: Instantaneous
> Effect: Teleports caster to sanctuary
>
> Similar to Teleport, but always returns the
> cleric and carried equipment to a prepared
> sanctuary meditation room, regardless of
> distance.

## Polymorph Other

> **Polymorph Other**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 8 **R:** near (~18 m / 60 ft)  
> **T:** one living creature **D:** permanent until dispelled
>
> You rewrite the physical and behavioral template of a living target, reshaping it into another creature form. Unlike self-transformation, the subject gains the complete profile of the new form — all special abilities, immunities, and innate behavioral tendencies. The new form's Hit Dice cannot exceed twice the target's original. The new form cannot be a specific named individual.
>
> The target makes a Save vs. Spells; on failure, the transformation is permanent until dispelled. The behavioral shift is real: a target reshaped into a predator begins to think and act like one, with personality drift deepening over time.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — the target takes a −2 penalty to its Save; x4 — the referee may rule that a long-held transformation resists Dispel Magic alone and requires additional effort to restore the original identity.
>
> See also: `Polymorph Self` for the caster-safe variant.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [transformation]
>   [control]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: Polymorph Others
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Polymorph Others
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Polymorph Others
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Polymorph Other; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Polymorph Others
> Range: 60'
> Duration: Permanent until dispelled
> Effect: One living creature
>
> This spell transforms one living creature
> into another type of creature. The new
> form may not have more Hit Dice than
> twice the original creature's Hit Dice.
> The target gains ALL of the new form's
> special abilities and behavioral tendencies
> (unlike Polymorph Self). A Save vs.
> Spells is allowed; failure means the
> transformation is permanent until
> dispelled. The new form cannot be a
> specific named individual.

  <div class="power-return">
    &nbsp;&nbsp;
    <a class="js-back-link" href="#chapter-06-power-index-anchor" aria-label="Back to previous page">
      ↩ Back
    </a>
  </div>

</div>

## Growth of Animal

> **Growth of Animal**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 6 **R:** far (~36 m / 120 ft)  
> **T:** one normal or giant animal **D:** 12 turns (~2 hours)
>
> You amplify one beast's physical scale and muscle output, doubling its size and drastically increasing carrying capacity and striking power. The target deals double normal damage, carries roughly double its usual load, and otherwise remains the same creature mentally and behaviorally.
>
> The power does not improve Armor, hit points, or intelligent/fantastic creature profiles.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — extend the effect to one additional nearby eligible animal; x4 — the enlarged target also gains advantage on tests of force, hauling, or trampling pressure.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [transformation]
>   [buff]
>   [animal]
>   [cleric]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: Growth of Animal
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Growth of Animal
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Growth of Animal; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Growth of Animal
> Range: 120'
> Duration: 12 turns
> Effect: Doubles the size of one animal
>
> This spell doubles the size of one normal
> or giant animal. The animal has twice its
> normal strength, inflicts double normal
> damage, and may carry twice its normal
> encumbrance. Behavior, Armor Class, and
> hit points do not change.

## Stone to Flesh

> **Stone to Flesh**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 12 **R:** far (~36 m / 120 ft)  
> **T:** one petrified creature or up to a 10 ft cube of stone **D:** permanent
>
> You reverse petrification or transmute a bounded volume of inert stone into flesh. Most often this restores a creature turned to stone, including body function and carried state at referee call.
>
> _Reverse — Flesh to Stone:_ Target one living creature and all carried equipment. The target may Save vs. Turn to Stone to resist.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — stabilize a freshly restored target against shock, poison, or similar collapse effects for 1 turn; x4 — also remove one secondary petrification side-effect (hairline fractures, sensory lag, mineral scarring) if present.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [transformation]
>   [restoration]
>   [reversible]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: Stone to Flesh
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Stone to Flesh
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Stone to Flesh; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Stone to Flesh*
> Range: 120'
> Duration: Permanent
> Effect: One creature or object
>
> This spell turns any one statue (or up to
> 10' x 10' x 10' of stone) to flesh, often
> used to restore a petrified victim. The
> reverse, Flesh to Stone, turns one living
> creature and carried equipment to stone;
> the victim may Save vs. Turn to Stone.

## Metal to Wood

> **Metal to Wood**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 14 **R:** far (~36 m / 120 ft)  
> **T:** metal item(s) totaling up to 50 cn per user Level **D:** permanent
>
> You transmute selected metal into dead wood. Converted armor falls away, and converted weapons become nonmagical wooden equivalents.
>
> Magical metal is highly resistant (typically 90% chance to resist). The change is permanent and not reversed by ordinary dispel procedures.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - permit selective shaping so converted material remains structurally useful (bridge braces, braces, wedges); x4 - affect one additional separate target cluster within range.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [transformation]
>   [material]
>   [druid]
>   [high-tier]

osr:
> Metal to Wood
> Range: 120'
> Duration: Permanent
> Effect: Changes metal into dead wood
>
> Converts up to five pounds of metal per
> caster level into wood. Magical metal has
> strong resistance. Converted armor and
> weapons lose their normal function.

## Dissolve

> **Dissolve**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 10 **R:** far (~70 m / 240 ft)  
> **T:** soil/rock volume up to 3,000 sq ft surface area and 10 ft depth **D:** 3-18 days
>
> You transmute ground or stone (not finished constructions) into deep mud, creating broad terrain denial and movement collapse.
>
> Traversing the zone drops movement to a fraction of normal and may trap targets pending saves or extraction.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - shape the dissolved zone into tactical channels, pits, or segmented lanes; x4 - hold edge stability so selected friendly routes remain passable.

tags:

> Duration: 3-18 days
> Effect: Liquefies 3,000 square feet
>
> Changes a large volume of soil or rock
> into mud, severely slowing movement and
> potentially trapping creatures.

## Warp Wood

>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 4 **R:** far (~70 m / 240 ft)  
> **T:** wooden weapons/tools scaled by user Level capacity **D:** permanent
>
> You twist and deform wooden weapons and selected wooden implements, often rendering them unusable.
>
> Capacity scales by item size-equivalency: arrows, spears/javelins/wands, and larger wood gear consume different shares of effect budget. Some magical wooden items may resist.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - include one additional category of wooden battlefield object (shields, hafts, bows); x4 - shape a targeted bend that makes repair difficult without full workshop support.

tags:

## Polymorph Any Object

> **Polymorph Any Object**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 16 **R:** very far (~72 m / 240 ft)  
> **T:** one creature or object **D:** see duration by kingdom (below)
>
> You reshape the fundamental form of a creature or object at range. If the target is structural (a section of wall, a ship panel), the effect reaches up to a 10' × 10' × 10' volume. Against unwilling living targets, allow a Save vs. Spells at –4; if the save succeeds, the form holds.
>
> Duration depends on how far the change crosses the three kingdoms (animal, vegetable, mineral):
>
> - **Same kingdom** (animal → animal, etc.): permanent until dispelled
> - **Adjacent kingdoms** (animal ↔ vegetable, vegetable ↔ mineral): 1 hour per user Level
> - **Opposite kingdoms** (animal ↔ mineral): 1 turn per user Level
>
> This power cannot affect a creature whose Hit Dice exceed twice the user's Level. Polymorphed creatures retain their hp and age; they do not automatically become friendly.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — extend the volume limit to a 20' cube for structural targets; x4 — the target's Save penalty increases to –8 and a permanent-category change also strips the target's innate magical abilities for the duration.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [transformation]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Polymorph Any Object
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Polymorph Any Object
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Polymorph Any Object; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Polymorph Any Object
> Range: 240'
> Duration: Permanent (same kingdom) / 1 hr per level (adjacent) / 1 turn per level (opposite)
> Effect: Changes form of one creature or object
>
> Targets objects and creatures; if structural, up to 10'×10'×10'. Save
> vs. Spells at –4. Duration by kingdom change. Cannot affect creatures
> with >2× caster HD. Polymorphed creatures are not automatically
> friendly and retain hp and age.

  <div class="power-return">
    &nbsp;&nbsp;
    <a class="js-back-link" href="#chapter-06-power-index-anchor" aria-label="Back to previous page">
      ↩ Back
    </a>
  </div>

</div>

<div class="power-card" markdown="1">

## Shapechange

> **Shapechange**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 18 **R:** self  
> **T:** self **D:** 40 turns (~4 hours)
>
> You dissolve all constraint of form. For the duration you may assume the shape of any creature or object you have observed, provided the new form does not exceed 40 feet in any dimension or 4,000 cn in mass. You may shift again each round without breaking the duration.
>
> You gain the physical capabilities, movement modes, armor, and natural attacks of whatever form you hold — including flight, aquatic breathing, limb count, and natural venom if applicable. You retain your own mind, memories, and languages.
>
> Unlike polymorph, you are not limited by form-family or kingdom distance. Any observed form is available.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — extend the duration to 80 turns; x4 — the size limit rises to 80 feet / 8,000 cn.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:fantascience]
>   [storage:item]
>   [transformation]
>   [self]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Shapechange
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Shapechange
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Shapechange; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Shapechange
> Range: Self
> Duration: 40 turns
> Effect: Assume any creature or object form up to 40 ft / 4,000 cn
>
> Caster may assume any observed form within size limits, shifting each
> round if desired. Gain full capabilities of assumed form. Retain own
> mind. Source: Master Set artifact table D2 (M9); RC ninth level list.
> [Synthesis: capability inheritance and form-shift cadence extrapolated
> from artifact entry and BECMI polymorph family doctrine.]

## Stoneform

> **Stoneform**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 12 **R:** touch
> **T:** created stone mass up to 1,000 cubic feet **D:** permanent
>
> You create and shape a contiguous mass of mundane stone in any supported geometry (wall, stair, block, statue, or structural component). Complexity determines casting time, from 1 round for simple forms up to 12 turns for highly detailed work.
>
> Later castings by the same user can modify prior Stoneform works until locked. Separate castings can join seamlessly, enabling large durable construction.
>
> The result is permanent non-dispellable stone and must be supported by ground or equivalent structure.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - treat the created structure as reinforced for collapse checks. x4 - create precision-fit architectural detail in one cast without later refinement passes.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [creation]
>   [earth]
>   [construction]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Stoneform
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Stoneform; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Stoneform
> Range: Touch
> Duration: Permanent
> Effect: Creates 1,000 cubic feet of stone
>
> Creates solid stone in chosen shape; casting time scales with complexity.
> Stone is permanent, non-dispellable, and may be seamlessly joined to prior Stoneform structures.

</div>

## Woodform

> **Woodform**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 10 **R:** touch
> **T:** created wood mass up to 1,000 cubic feet **D:** permanent
>
> You create and shape a contiguous mass of mundane wood in chosen geometry (wall, beam, hull member, stair, or carved structure). Complexity sets casting time: simple in 1 round, precision works up to 12 turns.
>
> Later woodform castings can modify prior woodform creations until locked. Separate castings can join seamlessly to expand structures.
>
> Created wood is permanent and non-dispellable, though it remains vulnerable to normal fire, force, and destruction.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - grant reinforced grain structure for durability checks. x4 - create precision maritime or architectural fittings in a single cast.

> Duration: Permanent
> Effect: Creates 1,000 cubic feet of wood
>
> Creates permanent non-dispellable wood in chosen shape.
> Casting time scales with complexity and later castings may refine earlier woodform structures.

## Ironform

> **Ironform**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 14 **R:** touch
> **T:** created iron mass up to 500 sq ft at up to 2" thickness **D:** permanent
>
> You create and shape contiguous iron as walling, reinforcement, gates, plates, or sculpted structural pieces. Geometry is flexible and not restricted to vertical placement.
>
> Casting time scales by complexity. Later ironform casts can refine prior ironform creations until locked, and separate castings can join seamlessly.
>
> Created iron is permanent and non-dispellable, though still vulnerable to disintegrate-grade effects and rust-monster corrosion.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - increase maximum thickness in focused segments. x4 - produce precision mechanical-grade shaping for one static component.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]

> Ironform
> Range: Touch
> Duration: Permanent
> Effect: Creates 500 square feet of iron
>
> Creates permanent iron forms with complexity-based casting times.
> Later casts can refine and seamlessly join earlier ironform work.

## Statue

> **Statue**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 14 **R:** self
> **T:** caster and carried nonliving gear **D:** 2 turns per user Level
>
> You can phase between normal form and statue form once per round. In statue form you are immobile but heavily protected: strong armor state, no breathing requirement, and immunity to many mundane hazards.
>
> You can maintain concentration on already-active effects while in statue form, but cannot cast new powers.
>
> Magical weapons and certain spells still damage you normally.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - gain one reactive shift outside your turn when directly targeted. x4 - statue form can anchor one adjacent ally in partial cover stance.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [defense]
>   [transformation]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Statue
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Statue
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Statue; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Statue
> Range: 0 (magic-user only)
> Duration: 2 turns per level of the caster
> Effect: Allows caster to turn to stone
>
> Caster may shift to or from statue form once per round.
> Statue form is highly resistant to mundane harm but remains vulnerable to magical attacks.

# Mind and Emotion

Use these for mental influence, charm effects, fear, suggestion, and emotional manipulation. Covers enchantment, compulsion, and mental domination.

<div class="power-card" markdown="1">

## Charm Person

> **Charm Person**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 2 **R:** far (~35 m / 120 ft)  
> **T:** one living humanoid-scale target **D:** until broken or resisted free
>
> You impose a persuasive best-friend bond on a humanoid-scale target. The target makes an Aura save; on failure, it treats you as a trusted ally and will usually follow spoken guidance framed as friendly suggestion. Commands that sharply violate the target's habits, loyalties, or nature may be resisted, and no target can be compelled to kill itself.
>
> The charm breaks immediately if you directly attack the target. Referees should allow repeat saves on an Intelligence-based cadence measured in days, weeks, or months rather than rounds.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — extend the charm to one additional nearby eligible target; x4 — you may issue one brief command silently through the charm-link once per scene.
>
> See also: `Hero's Goldenmouth` in the SDM Powers Index for a related rhetoric-forward influence variant.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [mental]
>   [social]
>   [control]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Basic Rules; spell: Charm Person
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Charm Person
>   - file: Synthetic_Dream_Machine_04_Powers_Index.md; related: Hero's Goldenmouth
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Charm Person; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Charm Person
> Range: 120'
> Duration: See below
> Effect: One living "person" (see below)
>
> This spell will only affect humans, demi-
> humans, and certain other creatures.
> The victim is allowed a Saving Throw vs.
> Spells. If the Saving Throw is successful,
> the spell has no effect. If it is failed, the
> victim will believe that the magic-user is
> its "best friend," and will try to defend
> the magic-user against any threat,
> whether real or imagined. The victim is
> "Charmed."
>
> If the magic-user can speak a lan-
> guage that the Charmed victim under-
> stands, the magic-user may give orders
> to the victim. These orders should
> sound like suggestions, as if ")ut be-
> tween friends." These orders will usually
> be obeyed, but orders that are contrary
> to the victim's nature (alignment and
> habits) may be resisted. A victim will
> refuse to obey if ordered to kill itself.
>
> The Charm is automatically broken if
> t h e magic-user attacks t h e victim,
> whether by spell or by weapon.

## Sleep

> **Sleep**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 2 **R:** far (~70 m / 240 ft)  
> **T:** one group of low-level creatures in a 40 ft / 12 m area **D:** 4d4 turns
>
> You flood a local zone with noospheric sedation. Creatures of modest Level in the area collapse into magical sleep with no save if they fall under the effect threshold; affected targets remain asleep until the duration ends or they are awakened by force, loud disturbance, or injury.
>
> High-level or unusually resilient targets are unaffected.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — increase affected creature threshold or include one additional nearby cluster; x4 — sleeping targets wake disoriented and lose reactions until end of their first round awake.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [mental]
>   [control]
>   [disable]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Basic Rules; spell: Sleep
>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: Sleep
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Sleep
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Sleep; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Sleep
> Range: 240'
> Duration: 4d4 turns
> Effect: 2-16 Hit Dice of creatures
>
> This spell puts creatures into magical
> sleep. Low-level creatures are affected
> first; higher-level creatures may be immune
> if the total effect is exhausted.

## Confusion

> **Confusion**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 8 **R:** far (~35 m / 120 ft)  
> **T:** creatures in a 20 ft / 6 m radius area **D:** 12 rounds
>
> You shatter local coherence with contradictory impulse-noise. Affected creatures make an Aura save each round; on failure they lose tactical clarity and act erratically (hesitation, wandering, random target fixation, or self-sabotaging choices as referee adjudicates).
>
> Coordinated formations degrade quickly while this field holds.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - increase area to 30 ft / 9 m radius; x4 - failed saves also strip reactions until start of the target's next turn.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [mental]
>   [control]
>   [debuff]

>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Confusion
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Confusion; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Confusion
> Range: 120'
> Duration: 12 rounds
> Effect: Creatures in an area
>
> This spell scrambles intent and judgment,
> causing affected targets to behave in
> erratic and tactically unsound ways.

## Feeblemind

> **Feeblemind**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 10 **R:** far (~35 m / 120 ft)  
> **T:** one intelligent creature capable of spell use **D:** permanent until cured
>
> You collapse higher cognition into near-animal baseline. The target makes an Aura save with major penalty if currently casting or preparing powers. On failure, the target loses advanced reasoning, speech complexity, and practical power use until restored by high-tier recovery procedures.
>
> This is a severe campaign-level effect and should be treated as major consequence magic.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - impose lingering psychic static even on successful save (temporary penalties for 1 turn); x4 - require two successful recovery checks during restoration to fully clear the effect.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [mental]
>   [debuff]
>   [dangerous]

>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Feeblemind
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Feeblemind; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Feeblemind
> Range: 120'
> Duration: Permanent
> Effect: One spellcasting-capable creature
>
> This spell destroys higher reasoning and
> spell use capability until reversed by strong
> restorative magic.

## Charm Monster

> **Charm Monster**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 8 **R:** far (~35 m / 120 ft)  
> **T:** one creature (or 3d6 creatures of 3 HD or less) **D:** special (see below)
>
> You extend dominion over nonhuman minds. Any living creature except undead may be targeted — not just humanoids. Creatures of 3 HD or fewer are affected in groups; a single creature of 4+ HD may be targeted alone. Each target may resist with a Save vs. Spells.
>
> A charmed creature treats you as a trusted ally. It won't obey obviously self-destructive commands but interprets orders generously. The charm persists until dispelled or until the creature's natural resistance erodes it (periodic Save; referee determines frequency based on creature type and improbable orders).
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — impose a -2 penalty on the target's Save; x4 — suspend further periodic Saves for the first 10 days while the deep-trust window holds.
>
> See also: `Charm Person` in this chapter and `Hero's Goldenmouth` (Our Golden Age) for social-capture descendants.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:fantascience]
>   [storage:item]
>   [charm]
>   [creature-control]
>   [mind]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: Charm Monster
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Charm Monster
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Charm Monster; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Charm Monster
> Range: 120'
> Duration: Special
> Effect: One or more living creatures
>
> This spell effect is identical to that of
> a charm person spell, but any creature
> except an undead may be affected. If the
> victims have 3 Hit Dice or less, 3-18 may
> be charmed. Otherwise, only one monster
> will be affected. Each victim may make a
> Saving Throw vs. Spells to avoid the effects.

## Dance

> **Dance**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 16 **R:** touch  
> **T:** one living creature **D:** 3 to 7 rounds by caster tier
>
> You impose a compulsive motor loop on one touched victim. The target receives no save, cannot attack, cast, use spell-like abilities, or flee, and instead staggers through forced dance movements.
>
> While affected, the victim suffers a -4 penalty to saving throws and a +4 penalty to Armor Class.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - extend the routine by one additional round at your current tier; x4 - the first attempted external disruption of the dance fails unless backed by explicit countermagic or physical separation from you.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [mind]
>   [compulsion]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Dance
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Dance
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Dance; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Dance
> Range: Touch
> Duration: 3 or more rounds
> Effect: Causes 1 victim to dance
>
> A touched victim gets no saving throw, cannot
> attack, cast, or flee, suffers -4 to saves and
> +4 to Armor Class, and remains affected for
> 3 to 7 rounds based on caster level.

## Mass Charm

> **Mass Charm**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 16 **R:** far (~36 m / 120 ft)  
> **T:** up to 30 HD of creatures in range **D:** special (by Intelligence, as Charm Person)
>
> You broadcast a wide-band compulsion signal, laying a charm effect on every creature in range up to 30 HD total. Each affected creature must Save vs. Spells at –2 or fall under your charm. The spell cannot affect any single creature of 31+ HD or Levels.
>
> Each charm endures according to the victim's Intelligence as per the standard charm-person table. If you attack one charmed creature, only that creature's charm breaks automatically. Others may make a fresh Save when they witness the attack, but their charms are otherwise unaffected.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — extend the total target cap to 50 HD; x4 — the saving throw penalty becomes –4 and charmed creatures also take –2 to any check that would let them reinterpret your commands.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:fantascience]
>   [storage:item]
>   [control]
>   [charm]
>   [mind]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Mass Charm
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Mass Charm
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Mass Charm; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Mass Charm*
> Range: 120'
> Duration: Special (as charm person spell)
> Effect: 30 Levels of creatures
>
> Affects up to 30 HD at once at –2 to Save. Cannot affect creatures
> of 31+ HD. Duration by Intelligence as per charm person.
> Reverse: Remove Charm (see companion entry).

  <div class="power-return">

## Remove Charm

> **Remove Charm**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 16 **R:** far (~36 m / 120 ft)  
> **T:** a 20' × 20' × 20' volume **D:** instant (charm removal); 1 turn (object suppression)
>
> You sweep all charm effects from a defined volume, unfailingly removing every active charm regardless of source or caster level. No save is allowed against this purge.
>
> In addition, the purge leaves a suppression field in the target volume for 1 turn: any object within the area that would normally generate charm effects cannot do so until the turn expires.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — also clear one charm-like domination or compulsion effect per user Level present in the volume; x4 — extend the suppression field duration to 1 turn per user Level.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:fantascience]
>   [storage:item]
>   [removal]
>   [charm]
>   [mind]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Mass Charm (reverse: Remove Charm)
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Remove Charm
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Remove Charm; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Remove Charm* (reverse of Mass Charm)
> Range: 120'
> Duration: Instant / 1 turn (object suppression)
> Effect: 20' x 20' x 20' volume
>
> Unfailingly removes all charm effects in the volume.
> Prevents objects in the area from generating charm effects for 1 turn.
> RC indexes as a standalone MU 8 entry.

  <div class="power-return">
    &nbsp;&nbsp;

      ↩ Back
    </a>

## Snake Charm

> **Snake Charm**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 4 **R:** far (~18 m / 60 ft)  
> **T:** snakes totaling up to 1 HD per user Level **D:** 2-5 rounds if hostile; 2-5 turns otherwise
>
> You impose a narrow harmonic charm on nearby snakes. Affected serpents rise, sway, and cease aggression. No save is allowed. If the snakes were actively attacking, the calm only lasts briefly; otherwise, the entrancement can hold much longer.
>
> Charmed snakes do not become loyal servants. If attacked, they defend themselves, and when the effect ends they return to ordinary reaction behavior.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — include one additional small snake cluster beyond the normal HD cap; x4 — while the charm holds, you may guide the snakes' movement within the local area as a simple procession.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [control]
>   [animal]
>   [charm]
>   [cleric]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: Snake Charm
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Snake Charm
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Snake Charm; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Snake Charm
> Range: 60'
> Duration: 2-5 rounds or 2-5 turns
> Effect: Charms 1 HD of snakes per caster level
>
> The cleric may charm 1 Hit Die of snakes
> per level, with no Saving Throw. The
> snakes rise and sway but do not attack
> unless attacked. The duration is shorter if
> used on attacking snakes and longer
> otherwise.

## Magic Jar

> **Magic Jar**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 10 **R:** near (~9 m / 30 ft)  
> **T:** one prepared vessel and one creature within 120 ft of that vessel **D:** special (until return, disruption, or destruction)
>
> You project your life-force into a prepared inanimate vessel, then attempt body possession through it. A target may Save vs. Spells to resist possession. On failure, you control that body while the target's life-force is displaced into the vessel.
>
> While possessing a host, you can perform normal physical actions but cannot access host-exclusive special abilities unless the referee allows limited overlap. `Dispel Evil` forces your life-force out of the host and back into the vessel.
>
> Catastrophic states matter: if the vessel is destroyed while your essence is inside it, you die. If destroyed while you are in a host, you are stranded in that host body.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — gain a brief synchronization window that reduces host-action penalties for the first turn; x4 — once per possession, force the host to reroll a successful resistance check and keep the worse result.
>
> See also: `Magic Jar` in the SDM Powers Index for an existing exact-name rendition.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [mind]
>   [possession]
>   [dangerous]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: Magic Jar
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Magic Jar
>   - file: Synthetic_Dream_Machine_04_Powers_Index.md; related: Magic Jar
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Magic Jar; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Magic Jar
> Range: 30'
> Duration: See below
> Effect: Possess one body
>
> The caster's life-force enters an inanimate
> vessel, then may attempt to possess one
> creature within 120' of the vessel. Targets
> Save vs. Spells to resist. If possession
> succeeds, the victim's life-force is placed in
> the jar. Destroying the jar can kill or strand
> the caster depending on current state.

## Quest

> **Quest**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 10 **R:** near (~9 m / 30 ft)  
> **T:** one living creature **D:** special (until fulfilled or removed)
>
> You bind a target to a declared mission imperative. On a failed Save vs. Spells, the target is compelled to undertake the assigned task and remains under geas-like pressure until completion.
>
> The command must be difficult but achievable; impossible or outright suicidal directives fail to bind. Refusal to pursue the quest invokes an ongoing curse defined by referee consequence doctrine.
>
> _Reverse — Remove Quest:_ Attempts to break an unwanted quest-binding or quest-linked curse, with success chance scaling by relative caster level.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - seal the quest with one explicit taboo clause that intensifies penalties on breach; x4 - bind up to two linked milestones that must be completed in sequence.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [mind]
>   [compulsion]
>   [curse]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Companion Set; spell: Quest
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Quest
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Quest; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Quest*
> Range: 30'
> Duration: Special
> Effect: Compels one living creature
>
> Forces one target to perform a specific
> task unless it saves. Refusal to continue
> the quest imposes a curse. Reverse form
> removes quest effects with level-based
> chance of success.

  <div class="power-return">
    &nbsp;&nbsp;
    <a class="js-back-link" href="#chapter-06-power-index-anchor" aria-label="Back to previous page">
      ↩ Back
    </a>
  </div>

</div>


<div class="power-card" markdown="1">

## Charm Plant

> **Charm Plant**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 14 **R:** far (~36 m / 120 ft)
> **T:** one tree, 6 bushes, 12 shrubs, or 24 small plants **D:** up to 6 months (seasonal limits)
>
> You bind local plants into cooperative behavior. Charmed flora obeys feasible commands: obstructing routes, entangling intruders, screening approaches, and similar station-keeping responses.
>
> Plant-like monsters may attempt an Aura save to resist. Ordinary plants do not save.
>
> Charm ends at winter dormancy unless sustained by additional magic.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - increase controlled footprint category by one step. x4 - maintain activity through one dormancy interval with explicit dangerous backlash risk.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [control]
>   [nature]
>   [charm]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Companion Set; spell: Charm Plant
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Charm Plant
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Charm Plant; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Charm Plant
> Range: 120'
> Duration: 6 months (see below)
> Effect: Charms one tree or more smaller plants
>
> Plants obey caster commands within plant capability. Plant-like monsters may save.
> Effect ends on dispel or winter dormancy.

# Veils and Influence

Use these for denial, concealment, and social/battlefield control rather than direct damage. Covers illusion, invisibility, blindness, and misdirection.

<div class="power-card" markdown="1">

## Invisibility

> **Invisibility**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 4 **R:** touch  
> **T:** self or one willing creature **D:** until broken (attack/cast/offensive disruption)
>
> You bend light and attention around the target. Carried and worn items also turn invisible. Items become visible when dropped or removed from possession. The effect ends if the target attacks or casts an offensive power; passive movement and stealth do not break it.
>
> Invisible creatures can still be found by contact, area effects, and dedicated detection powers.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — include one adjacent willing creature at cast time; x4 — convert to a 10 ft / 3 m radius invisibility field anchored to one bearer.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [illusion]
>   [focus]
>   [imbued]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Basic Rules; spell: Invisibility
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Invisibility
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Invisibility; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Invisibility
> Range: 240'
> Duration: Permanent until broken
> Effect: One creature or object
>
> This spell will make any one creature or
> object invisible. When a creature be-
> comes invisible, all items carried and
> worn also become invisible. Any invisible
> item becomes visible again when it leaves
> the creature's possession (dropped, set
> down, etc.). If the magic-user makes an
> object invisible that is not being carried
> or worn, it will become visible again
> when touched by any living creature. An
> invisible creature will remain invisible
> until he or she attacks or casts any spell.
> A light source (such as a torch) may be
> made invisible, but the light given off
> will always remain visible.

  <div class="power-return">

      ↩ Back
    </a>

## Projected Image

> **Projected Image**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 12 **R:** far (~70 m / 240 ft)  
> **T:** one full-scale visual proxy of the caster **D:** 6 turns (~1 hour)
>
> You emit a stable duplicate image of yourself at range. It persists without concentration and is visually indistinguishable from you unless physically tested.
>
> While the image is active, your spellcasting appears to originate from the image, but you must still maintain true line of sight to valid targets. Missile fire and spell effects seem to pass through harmlessly; direct touch or melee contact collapses the projection.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — image can produce synchronized voice and ambient casting signatures, making the proxy harder to challenge; x4 — allow one short reposition of the image each round within a local area.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [illusion]
>   [decoy]
>   [control]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: Projected Image
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Projected Image
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Projected Image; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Projected Image
> Range: 240'
> Duration: 6 turns
> Effect: Creates one image
>
> This spell creates an image of the caster
> up to 240' away. The image cannot be
> distinguished from the original except by
> touch. Spells cast seem to come from the
> image, though the caster must still see the
> target. Touch or melee contact ends it.

  <div class="power-return">

## Invisibility 10' Radius

> **Invisibility 10' Radius**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 6 **R:** self  
> **T:** all willing creatures within a 10 ft / 3 m radius field **D:** until broken by offensive action
>
> You anchor a mobile concealment bubble to yourself. Allied creatures in the field become invisible together as long as they remain within radius. Carried gear is also concealed; dropped items become visible.
>
> If any affected creature makes an offensive attack or launches an overtly hostile power, that creature's concealment breaks immediately.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - expand radius to 15 ft / 4.5 m; x4 - affected creatures retain concealment for 1 round after briefly stepping outside the bubble.
>
> See also: `Yellow Cloud` in the SDM Powers Index for an area-obscuration cousin.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [illusion]
>   [focus]
>   [imbued]
>   [group]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: Invisibility 10' radius
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Invisibility 10' Radius
>   - file: Synthetic_Dream_Machine_04_Powers_Index.md; related: Yellow Cloud
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Invisibility 10' Radius; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Invisibility 10' Radius
> Range: 120'
> Duration: Permanent until broken
> Effect: All creatures in 10' radius
>
> This spell extends invisibility to all creatures
> within ten feet of the target point or anchor,
> with the same break conditions as standard
> invisibility when hostile action is taken.

## Mirror Image

> **Mirror Image**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 4 **R:** self  
> **T:** self plus decoy image cluster **D:** 6 turns (~1 hour)
>
> You split your visual profile into multiple shimmering duplicates that track your motion and mislead incoming strikes. When an attack would hit you, roll to determine whether it strikes a false image instead. Each destroyed image dissipates in a flare of static light.
>
> The effect deceives sight-driven targeting; blind area effects still threaten you normally.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - increase starting duplicate count; x4 - once per round, force an attacker to reroll a successful hit against you.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [illusion]
>   [defense]
>   [focus]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: Mirror Image
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Mirror Image
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Mirror Image; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Mirror Image
> Range: 0
> Duration: 6 turns
> Effect: Caster and 1d4+1 images
>
> This spell creates duplicate images around
> the caster that mimic movement and cause
> attackers to strike false targets before the
> real caster can be hit.

## Phantasmal Force

> **Phantasmal Force**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 4 **R:** far (~70 m / 240 ft)  
> **T:** one scene-scale illusion construct **D:** focus, up to 12 turns (~2 hours)
>
> You fabricate a controlled illusion of creature, object, terrain feature, or event pattern. The construct can carry sight/sound texture strong enough to redirect movement, bait reactions, or cover an extraction.
>
> Targets interacting closely with the illusion may test Aura to disbelieve specific elements.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - add heat/light or scent cues for stronger realism; x4 - split the phantasm into two coordinated false elements in the same scene.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]

> Phantasmal Force
> Range: 240'
> Duration: Concentration
> Effect: Visual/sensory illusion
>
> This spell creates a believable illusion the
> caster controls, limited by concentration and
> by what observers can plausibly accept.

## Ventriloquism

> **Ventriloquism**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 2 **R:** far (~18 m / 60 ft)  
> **T:** one false voice origin point **D:** 2 turns (~20 minutes)
>
> You project your voice to another point in space, creating a convincing false speaker location. This can misdirect guards, trigger reactions, and support stealth repositioning when timed with ambient noise.
>
> Listeners may test Aura when the projected voice strongly conflicts with visible evidence.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - maintain two alternating false voice points; x4 - layer one additional simple auditory cue (footsteps, knock, whisper) with the speech.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [illusion]

osr:
> Ventriloquism
> Range: 60'
> Duration: 2 turns
> Effect: One false sound source
>
> This spell lets the caster make their voice
> seem to come from another location within
> range, misleading listeners about position.

## Levitate

> **Levitate**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 4 **R:** touch  
> **T:** self or one willing creature/object **D:** 6 turns + 1 turn per user Level
>
> You suspend the target in a stable vertical lift envelope. The target rises or descends at controlled speed and can hold a chosen elevation. Horizontal movement is limited to pushes, tethers, or environmental drift unless supported by another movement power.
>
> Levitation can be used for obstacle bypass, vertical recon, and controlled descent under load.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — include one additional adjacent willing target; x4 — grant slow directional drift control without external push.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [movement]
>   [utility]

osr:
> Levitate
> Range: Touch
> Duration: 6 turns + 1/level
> Effect: One creature or object
>
> This spell allows controlled vertical move-
> ment up or down. The subject can be held
> suspended at any chosen height for the
> duration.
