## Hold Person

> **Hold Person**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 4 **R:** far (~35 m / 120 ft)  
> **T:** one humanoid target, or up to four humanoid targets with overcharge **D:** up to 1 turn per user Level
>
> You lock motor intent with a rigid noospheric bind. Humanoid-scale targets make an Aura save; on failure they are paralyzed and cannot move, attack, or cast while held. Single-target casts apply a save penalty to represent focused binding pressure. Multi-target casts trade that penalty for wider coverage.
>
> This does not affect undead or very large creatures unless a specific entry says otherwise.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — target up to four humanoid creatures with standard saves; x4 — held targets cannot use reactions and move at zero speed on successful save until end of next turn.
>
> See also: `Hlod Person` in the SDM Powers Index for a related degeneration-pattern variant.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [control]
>   [mental]
>   [focus]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Basic Rules; spell: Hold Person
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Hold Person
>   - file: Synthetic_Dream_Machine_04_Powers_Index.md; related: Hlod Person
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Hold Person; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Hold Person
> Range: 180'
> Duration: 9 turns
> Effect: 1-4 persons (cleric's choice)
>
> This spell will affect any human, demi-
> human or human-like creature (such as
> bugbears, gnolls, gnomes, hobgoblins,
> kobolds, lizard men, ogres, orcs, pixies or
> sprites). It will not affect undead nor crea-
> tures of 5 Hit Dice or more. The victim(s)
> must make a Saving Throw vs. Spells or
> be paralyzed.
>
> This spell may be cast either at a single
> creature or at a group. If cast at a single
> creature, that victim must make a Saving
> Throw vs. Spells with a -2 penalty to the
> die roll. If cast at a group, it may affect up
> to 4 creatures, but no penalties apply to
> the Saving Throws.

  <div class="power-return">
    &nbsp;&nbsp;
    <a class="js-back-link" href="#chapter-06-power-index-anchor" aria-label="Back to previous page">
      ↩ Back
    </a>
  </div>

</div>

## Hold Monster

> **Hold Monster**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 10 **R:** far (~35 m / 120 ft)  
> **T:** 1–4 living creatures (not undead) **D:** 6 turns + 1 turn per user Level
>
> You clamp the motor-nerve field of any living creature — not just humanoids. Each target must pass a Save vs. Spells or stand paralyzed, unable to act or move. Targeting a single creature imposes a -2 penalty on their Save. Targeting a group affects 1–4 targets with no penalty applied.
>
> Paralysis ends when the duration expires, when dispelled, or when the reverse form Free Monster is invoked.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — extend duration to 12 turns + 1 per Level, or affect up to 6 targets in a group; x4 — apply a -4 penalty to Saves when targeting a single monster, completely seizing the creature's autonomous processes.
>
> See also: `Hold Person` in this chapter for the humanoid-only baseline version.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:fantascience]
>   [storage:item]
>   [hold]
>   [restraint]
>   [paralysis]
>   [battlefield]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: Hold Monster
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Hold Monster
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Hold Monster; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Hold Monster*
> Range: 120'
> Duration: 6 turns + 1 turn per level
> Effect: Paralyzes 1-4 creatures
>
> This spell has an effect identical to that
> of a hold person spell, but will affect any
> living creature (not undead). Each victim
> must make a Saving Throw vs. Spells or
> be paralyzed. Cast at a single creature:
> -2 penalty on the Save. Cast at a group:
> affects 1-4 creatures (caster's choice), no
> penalty. The reverse (free monster) removes
> paralysis from up to 4 victims of any
> hold spell.

  <div class="power-return">
    &nbsp;&nbsp;

      ↩ Back
    </a>

## Web

> **Web**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 4 **R:** far (~35 m / 120 ft)  
> **T:** one anchored 10 ft cube / layered strands across passage **D:** 48 turns (~8 hours) or until burned/cut free
>
> You extrude dense noospheric filament-webbing that anchors to walls, trees, rigging, or similar structure. Creatures entering or caught in the web must pass an Aura or Strength-style escape check (referee call) or become restrained.
>
> Fire destroys webs quickly but may injure trapped creatures.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - double covered volume or create two adjacent anchored webs; x4 - filament density imposes disadvantage on break attempts until first successful escape.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [control]
>   [area]
>   [utility]

osr:
> Web
> Range: 10'
> Duration: 48 turns
> Effect: A volume of sticky strands
>
> This spell creates strong sticky webs that
> fill an area and trap creatures. The web can
> be anchored to surfaces and is vulnerable
> to fire.

## Entangle

> **Entangle**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 4 **R:** near (~9 m / 30 ft)  
> **T:** ropes, vines, roots, or leather straps in range **D:** 1 round per user Level
>
> You animate rope-like material of living or once-living origin within range — roots, vines, leather ropes, plant-fibre cord, and similar. Roughly 50 feet of half-inch vine plus 5 feet per user Level can be affected.
>
> Animated material can be commanded to coil, loop, knot, tie, and the reverse of each. The material must be within 1 foot of whatever it is meant to bind. A creature attacked by animated entangle material may Save vs. Spells to avoid being bound.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — affect a second rope-like object simultaneously; x4 — a successfully knotted binding holds with the difficulty of a metal shackle (requires a tool or significant force to remove).

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [control]
>   [restraint]
>   [plant]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Entangle
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Entangle; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Entangle
> Range: 30'
> Duration: 1 round per level
> Effect: Controls ropes/vines
>
> Animates ~50 ft of vine/rope + 5 ft/level. Commands: coil, loop,
> knot, tie, and reverses. Material must be within 1 ft of target.
> Save vs. Spells to resist binding. RC-only provenance.

## Hallucinatory Terrain

> **Hallucinatory Terrain**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 8 **R:** far (~70 m / 240 ft)  
> **T:** one terrain feature or room-scale area **D:** until touched by an intelligent creature or dispelled
>
> You project a full sensory terrain falsehood over a real location: pits where none exist, false stairs, fake swamps, phantom groves, or concealed structures masked as harmless ground. The illusion holds as stable environmental deception until direct intelligent contact breaks the effect.
>
> This power changes perception, not physical topology.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — include ambient sound and temperature cues that reinforce the false terrain; x4 — first intelligent contact only weakens the illusion, requiring a deliberate second test to collapse it.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [illusion]
>   [terrain]
>   [control]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: Hallucinatory Terrain
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Hallucinatory Terrain
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Hallucinatory Terrain; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Hallucinatory Terrain
> Range: 240'
> Duration: Special
> Effect: Changes or hides terrain
>
> This spell creates the illusion of a terrain
> feature (indoors or outdoors), and may
> hide a real feature. The effect lasts until
> touched by an intelligent creature or until
> dispelled.

  <div class="power-return">

<div class="power-card" markdown="1">

## Geas

> **Geas**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 12 **R:** near (~9 m / 30 ft)  
> **T:** one creature **D:** until fulfilled, removed, or the subject dies
>
> You bind a target to a specific command constraint: perform an action, complete a mission, or abstain from a defined act. The command must be possible and not directly suicidal. The target may Save vs. Spells to resist.
>
> On failure, the compulsion persists until resolved. If the subject refuses compliance, escalating penalties apply at referee call (combat penalties, weakness, reduced capability, pain, or similar collapse effects).
>
> _Reverse — Remove Geas:_ This clears an existing geas. If the remover is lower Level than the original binder, removal may fail.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — apply a -2 penalty on the target's initial save; x4 — encode one clear completion condition that triggers immediate release when met.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [compulsion]
>   [binding]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: Geas
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Geas
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Geas; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Geas*
> Range: 30'
> Duration: Until completed or removed
> Effect: Compels one creature
>
> This spell compels a victim to perform or
> avoid a stated action. The target may Save
> vs. Spells. If ignored, penalties apply until
> the geas is obeyed or the victim dies.
> Dispel Magic and Remove Curse do not
> end geas. The reverse (Remove Geas) can
> remove it, with failure chance if the
> remover is lower level than the original
> caster.

## Massmorph

> **Massmorph**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 8 **R:** far (~70 m / 240 ft)  
> **T:** up to 100 man-sized creatures in a 240 ft diameter area **D:** until dispelled, dismissed, or a target leaves the zone
>
> You disguise a large group as orchard trees, dense woods, or similarly plausible vegetative cover. The illusion anchors to a broad area and can conceal the disguised creatures even from observers moving through that same space.
>
> Unwilling targets are unaffected. Moving within the affected area does not break the disguise, but leaving the area ends the false appearance for that creature.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — broaden the illusion to include camp gear, pack animals, and other nearby scene elements; x4 — add faint wind, shadow, and ambient rustle cues that make the false terrain harder to challenge casually.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [illusion]
>   [concealment]
>   [area]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: Massmorph
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Massmorph
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Massmorph; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Massmorph
> Range: 240'
> Duration: See below
> Effect: Causes illusion of trees
>
> This spell affects up to 100 human- or
> man-sized creatures in a 240' diameter,
> making them appear to be orchard trees
> or dense woods. Unwilling creatures are
> not affected. The illusion lasts until
> dispelled or ended by the caster, and a
> disguised creature loses the illusion only
> when it moves out of the affected area.

## Hold Animal

>
> You paralyze eligible animals in place. Each target may Save vs. Spells; on failure, it remains immobile for the duration.
>
> This power affects normal and giant animals, including summoned or controlled animals, but not fantastic creatures or beings above animal intelligence.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - impose a save penalty on first application; x4 - one failed target may also be rendered docile after paralysis ends for one brief scene.

## Obscure

> **Obscure**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 4 **R:** self  
> **T:** expanding mist cloud centered on caster (10 ft diameter and 1 ft height per user Level) **D:** 1 turn per user Level
>
> You raise a broad mist veil from the ground that blocks ordinary sight and confuses movement through the area.
>
> You and creatures able to see invisible can see dimly through the cloud. Others inside are effectively blind while within it.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - briefly detach part of the cloud as a drifting screen; x4 - concentrate particulate density into a near-wall segment that heavily impedes ranged attacks.
>
> See also: `Yellow Cloud` as a related SDM obscuration variant.

> blocks vision for most creatures and leaves
> them effectively blind within it.

## Mass Invisibility

> **Mass Invisibility**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 14 **R:** far (~70 m / 240 ft)
> **T:** creatures or objects within 60' square area **D:** sustained by standard invisibility break condition
>
> You apply invisibility across a broad group footprint. Each affected target becomes invisible with carried gear until attacking or casting, as per baseline invisibility doctrine.
>
> Capacity scales from a small set of huge creatures up to hundreds of human-scale targets.
>
> Reverse form, Appear, forces visibility in a local volume and suppresses renewed invisibility for one full turn.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - preserve concealment for one non-hostile interaction after movement. x4 - include astral-adjacent bleed-through silhouettes for one round of warning before full reveal.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [veil]
>   [invisibility]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Mass Invisibility
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Mass Invisibility
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Mass Invisibility; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Mass Invisibility
> Range: 240'
> Duration: Permanent until broken
> Effect: Creatures or objects in 60' square area
>
> Applies standard invisibility behavior to a large group.
> Reverse form reveals invisible targets in area and blocks new invisibility for 1 turn.

# Traversal and Mobility

Use these for route bypass, repositioning, and rapid scene transitions. Covers flight, teleportation, telekinesis, and dimensional access.

<div class="power-card" markdown="1">

## Fly

> **Fly**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 6 **R:** touch  
> **T:** self or one willing creature **D:** 1d6 turns + 1 turn per user Level
>
> You suspend the target in a controllable lift field. The target can move in any direction up to standard fast-travel flight pace (about 120 ft / round equivalent) and may stop to hover without falling. The recipient controls the movement after casting.
>
> Severe weather, anti-flight fields, and destabilizing interference may require an Aura or Endurance save to maintain control.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — grant one additional willing target; x4 — stabilize hover under heavy weather and allow one extra burden slot without speed loss.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [movement]
>   [imbued]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: Fly
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Fly
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Fly; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Fly
> Range: Touch
> Duration: 1-6 turns + 1 turn per level of
> the caster
> Effect: One creature may fly
>
> This spell allows the recipient (possibly the
> caster) to fly. The spell will permit move-
> ment in any direction and at any speed up
> to 360' per turn (120' per round) by mere
> concentration. The recipient may also stop
> and hover at any point (as a levitate spell),
> which does not require concentration.

## Swamp’s Gift (Water Breathing)

> **Swamp’s Gift (Water Breathing)**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 6 **R:** touch  
> **T:** self or one willing creature **D:** 1 day
>
> You tune the target's lungs and blood to dual-medium respiration. Until the effect ends, the target can breathe both water and air. In wetlands, marshes, and submerged terrain, movement penalties from waterlogged footing are ignored.
>
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — affect one additional willing adjacent target; x4 — all affected targets gain +2 Defense while submerged or in heavy wet cover.

>

> can freely move underwater in normal
> combat or exploration rounds.

## Lower Water

> **Lower Water**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 12 **R:** far (~70 m / 240 ft)  
> **T:** one contiguous water body area up to 10,000 sq ft **D:** 10 turns
>
> You depress local water level to half normal depth across a broad footprint, exposing channels, shoals, wreck zones, or crossings that are normally submerged.
>
> Vessels in the affected zone may ground. When the effect ends, returning surge can violently re-flood the zone and strip unsecured deck cargo or structures.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — extend duration to 20 turns; x4 — shape the lowered zone to preserve one controlled navigable channel through the exposed area.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [terrain]
>   [water]
>   [infrastructure]
>   [high-tier]

> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Lower Water; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Lower Water
> Range: 240'
> Duration: 10 turns
> Effect: Cuts depth to 1/2 normal
>
> This spell affects up to 10,000 square feet
> of water, lowering depth to half normal.
> Ships may become stuck. At duration end,
> the returning water can sweep decks and
> cause severe hull damage.

## Pass Plant

> **Pass Plant**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 10 **R:** self  
> **T:** caster transit between two same-type living trees **D:** instant
>
> You step into one living tree and emerge from another living tree of the same type within species-dependent range.
>
> Both trees must be large enough to contain you and must be alive. If either endpoint is dead or invalid, the transit fails.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - carry one adjacent willing creature through the transit; x4 - preserve a brief return-window link for one round.
>
> See also: `Linked Portals` as a broader SDM traversal cousin.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]

> Range: 0 (druid only)
> Duration: Instantaneous
> Effect: Short-range teleportation
>
> The druid enters one tree and exits another
> tree of the same type within set range
> limits. Both trees must be living and large
> enough for transit.

>

>
> Others cannot automatically use the opened path unless explicitly allowed by local ruling or overcharge effect.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - leave a brief stable route that one allied group can follow; x4 - permit conceal-and-observe posture within a large tree or growth cluster while effect lasts.

## Survival

> **Survival**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 18 **R:** touch  
> **T:** one creature **D:** 1 hour per user Level
>
> You shield the target from hostile nonmagical environmental conditions: extreme heat or cold, lack of air, vacuum exposure, and comparable natural hazards, including those found on other planes.
>
> While active, the protected target needs no air, food, water, or sleep. This does not block magical damage, poisons, breath weapons, attacks, or direct physical blows.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - extend the protection to one adjacent ally; x4 - preserve one shared environmental bubble for a small linked team under referee-approved formation constraints.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [survival]
>   [environment]
>   [high-tier]

> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Survival; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Survival
> Range: Touch
> Duration: One hour per level of the caster
> Effect: Protects one creature against all non-
> magical damage from the environment
>
> Protects against hostile environmental
> conditions, removes need for air, food,
> water, and sleep, and works against natural
> planar conditions as well.

## Transport Through Plants

>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>

> **T:** caster plus up to two willing creatures **D:** instant
>
> You use living plants as long-range transit gates. Enter one living plant and emerge from another living plant at the destination, anywhere on the same plane.
>
> Destination may be a specific known plant or a general area (with endpoint chosen by referee if unspecific). Both endpoints must be alive.
>
> Use limit: typically once per day.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - improve endpoint precision when destination is general rather than specific; x4 - keep a fragile return-trace open long enough for one immediate callback jump.

## Create Air

> **Create Air**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 6 **R:** immediate area / touch target
> **T:** 8,000 cubic feet area, one creature, one vehicle, or one sealed helm **D:** 1 hour per user Level
>
> You create breathable air where none exists. Cast on a room or area, the air stays in place. Cast on a creature, mount, helm, or vehicle, the air envelope travels with that target.
>
> The effect supports underwater and vacuum traversal, though poorly sealed gear can leak and reveal bubbles. This power does not neutralize poison gas unless that gas is part of normal breathable atmosphere.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - double breathable volume or include one additional linked target (rider and mount, or crew and vehicle). x4 - stabilize the air envelope against harsh pressure shifts for one scene.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [utility]
>   [traversal]
>   [air]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Create Air
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Create Air; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Create Air
> Range: immediate area
> Duration: 1 hour per level
> Effect: creates breathable air in 8,000 cubic feet (20' x 20' x 20')
>
> Air can be fixed to an area or made to travel with a creature, vehicle, or sealed helm.
> Useful underwater or in space transit. Does not block poison gases unless those gases are normal atmospheric components.

# Dimensional, Planar, and Exotic Access

Use these for planar travel, dimensional folding, portal creation, and access to the noosphere. Covers summoning, gating, and layer-shifting.

<div class="power-card" markdown="1">

## Dimension Door

> **Dimension Door**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 8 **R:** touch-origin (~10 ft / 3 m)  
> **T:** self or one creature within touch reach **D:** 1 round, then instant relocation
>
> You fold a short span of space and displace one creature to a chosen destination within roughly 360 ft / 110 m. The destination must either be known clearly or specified by workable directional distance. If the landing point is occupied by solid matter, the power fails rather than merging the target into stone.
>
> Unwilling targets may make an Aura save to resist the displacement.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — carry one willing adjacent companion; x4 — after arrival, the target may immediately take one move-only action without provoking reactions.
>
> See also: `Linked Portals` for a more stable portal-style traversal variant, and `Shadow Step` for a heritage short-hop analogue.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [movement]
>   [teleport]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: Dimension Door
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Dimension Door
>   - file: Synthetic_Dream_Machine_04_Powers_Index.md; related: Linked Portals
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Dimension Door; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Dimension Door
> Range: 10'
> Duration: 1 round
> Effect: Safely transports one creature
>
> This spell will transport one creature up to
> 10' from the caster, to a place up to 360'
> away. The caster picks the desired destina-
> tion. If the location is not known, distances
> not exceeding a total of 360' may be given.
> If this would cause the recipient to arrive at
> a location occupied by a solid object, the
> spell has no effect. An unwilling recipient
> may make a Saving Throw vs. Spells to
> avoid the effect.

  <div class="power-return">
    &nbsp;&nbsp;
    <a class="js-back-link" href="#chapter-06-power-index-anchor" aria-label="Back to previous page">
      ↩ Back
    </a>
  </div>

</div>

<div class="power-card" markdown="1">

## Teleport

> **Teleport**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 10 **R:** touch  
> **T:** self plus carried gear and optional willing companions by mass limit **D:** instant
>
> You execute long-range spatial transfer to a destination you know by direct familiarity, strong noospheric coordinates, or reliable ritual map-lock. Accuracy depends on destination certainty; poor data can produce off-target arrival, hazardous drift, or failed jump at referee call.
>
> Unwilling creatures cannot normally be carried unless a separate binding effect secures them first.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - include one additional willing companion of similar mass; x4 - improve arrival accuracy tier by one step when targeting uncertain destinations.
>
> See also: `Linked Portals` in the SDM Powers Index for stable route-anchored transit.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [movement]
>   [teleport]
>   [dangerous]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: Teleport
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Teleport
>   - file: Synthetic_Dream_Machine_04_Powers_Index.md; related: Linked Portals
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Teleport; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Teleport
> Range: 10'
> Duration: Instantaneous
> Effect: Caster and carried load
>
> This spell transports the caster (and possible
> companions/load) to a distant destination,
> with mishap risk if destination data is poor.

  <div class="power-return">
    &nbsp;&nbsp;

      ↩ Back
    </a>
  </div>

## Travel

> **Travel**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 16 **R:** self  
> **T:** caster plus touched companions by Level limit **D:** 1 turn per user Level
>
> You invoke a premium mobility suite that combines fast flight, adjacent-plane transition, and optional gaseous-transit mode.
>
> You may fly at high speed, bring additional touched companions based on your Level, and step across one nearby plane per turn. While the effect lasts, you may spend one full round to enter gaseous form; while gaseous you move faster, cannot cast or use items, and are harmed only by magic.
>
> Unwilling creatures may Save vs. Spells to resist being carried.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - improve companion capacity or transit speed for one segment; x4 - stabilize one multi-stage planar route so the whole group may shift without stagger drift.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [traversal]
>   [teleport]
>   [phase]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Travel
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Travel
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Travel; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Travel
> Range: 0
> Duration: One turn per level of the caster
> Effect: Allows aerial or gaseous travel
>
> Grants high-speed flight, adjacent-plane
> transition, and self-only gaseous form.
> Touched companions may be brought along
> based on caster level.

  <div class="power-return">
    &nbsp;&nbsp;
    <a class="js-back-link" href="#chapter-06-power-index-anchor" aria-label="Back to previous page">
      ↩ Back

<div class="power-card" markdown="1">

## Wish

> **Wish**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 18 **R:** special  
> **T:** one explicitly worded reality exception **D:** special
>
> You articulate a single high-tier exception to ordinary causality. The effect follows the exact wording used, not the caster's private intent.
>
> In routine use, Wish may safely duplicate any arcane spell of 8th level or lower or any clerical or druidic spell of 6th level or lower, subject to referee assent. Broader uses remain possible, but greedy, malicious, or structurally unstable wording invites distortion, partial success, rebound, or flat refusal.
>
> Wish cannot grant experience or levels. Harmful wishes allow the victim a Save vs. Spells; on success, half the effect rebounds on you, and you save at -4 to avoid that returning share.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - stabilize one carefully bounded substitution or utility exception, reducing hostile-interpretation drift; x4 - support one major but still limited rewrite such as temporary ability adjustment, costly treasure gain, or mitigation of a recent event, always at referee-controlled scope.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [ritual]
>   [reality]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Wish
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Wish
>   - file: Synthetic_Dream_Machine_04_Powers_Index.md; related: Big Wish
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Wish; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Wish
> Range: Special
> Duration: Special
> Effect: Special
>
> The single most powerful spell. Exact wording
> matters. It may duplicate many lower-level
> spells, but broader uses are referee-limited,
> cannot grant experience or levels, and may
> distort if phrased greedily or badly.

  <div class="power-return">
    &nbsp;&nbsp;

      ↩ Back
    </a>

## Gate

> **Gate**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 18 **R:** near (~9 m / 30 ft)  
> **T:** one portal to a named plane and, optionally, one named resident power **D:** 1 turn to an outer plane or 1d10 x 10 turns to a nearby plane
>
> You open a direct aperture to the Ethereal Plane, Astral Plane, one elemental plane, or one outer plane. Elemental and nearby-planar gates can remain open for extended intervals and may attract uninvited transit while active.
>
> Contact with an outer plane is substantially more dangerous. If you call a named great resident, that being or another responder may arrive and judge your reason for opening the way. Poor reasons tend to end badly.
>
> The reverse application closes a gate opened by this effect, and can also shut a nearby permanent gate such as an elemental vortex.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - stabilize the aperture and reduce stray-crossing risk during the first interval; x4 - hold the gate in clean alignment long enough for one declared transit sequence or controlled shutdown without turbulence.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [planar]
>   [portal]
>   [summon]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Gate
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Gate
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Gate; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Gate
> Range: 30'
> Duration: 1d10 x 10 turns or 1 turn
> Effect: Opens a portal to another plane
>
> Opens a direct planar connection. Nearby
> planes can stay open much longer; outer-plane
> contact is brief and dangerous, and may draw
> a powerful being in response. Reverse form
> closes compatible gates.

  <div class="power-return">

## Maze

> **Maze**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 18 **R:** near (~18 m / 60 ft)  
> **T:** one creature **D:** special (by Intelligence — 1d4 rounds to 1d6 turns)
>
> You fold the target into an indestructible astral maze, removing them from the scene entirely. No saving throw applies. The trapped creature navigates toward an exit; the time required depends on its Intelligence.
>
> | Target Intelligence | Escape Time |
> |---|---|
> | Non-to-Low (1–8) | 1d6 turns |
> | Average (9–12) | 2d20 rounds |
> | High (13–17) | 2d4 rounds |
> | Genius (18+) | 1d4 rounds |
>
> On escape, the creature reappears in exactly the spot from which it vanished. The maze is indestructible while active; no external spell can free the creature from the outside.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — add 1d6 rounds to the escape time regardless of Intelligence; x4 — the exit location randomizes within short range rather than returning the creature to the precise origin.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:fantascience]
>   [storage:item]
>   [exile]
>   [planar]
>   [dimensional]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Maze
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Maze
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Maze; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Maze
> Range: 60'
> Duration: See table (1d4 rounds to 1d6 turns based on Intelligence)
> Effect: Traps one creature in an indestructible astral maze
>
> No saving throw. Victim must find an exit; escape time depends on Intelligence.
> Returns to origin on escape. Cannot be dispelled from outside.

  <div class="power-return">

## Veilwalk (Pass-Wall)

>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 6 **R:** near (~9 m / 30 ft)  
> **T:** one solid wall-like barrier **D:** 3 turns
>
> You pull a passage seam through inert matter, opening a temporary tunnel through one wall segment up to 10 ft thick. The opening is wide enough for normal passage and then seals when duration ends.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — widen the opening to allow pack gear and mounts through safely; x4 — extend the wall-thickness limit to 20 ft.

## Timestop

> **Timestop**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 18 **R:** self  
> **T:** self **D:** 1+1d4 rounds
>
> You step outside normal time. For the duration, all other creatures and moving objects are frozen — they do not act, do not perceive, and cannot be directly harmed by the time-stopped caster. You move and act freely: casting spells, repositioning, setting up objects, preparing whatever you choose.
>
> At the end of the duration, time resumes exactly where it stopped for all other creatures. Any effects you set in motion (spells with delayed triggers, dropped objects, prepared positions) initiate normally from that moment.
>
> You cannot kill or directly damage a frozen creature during the stop — they are outside the normal flow of cause and effect. Setup, not slaughter, is the mode of this power.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — add 1d4 rounds to the rolled duration; x4 — you may bring one touching creature into the time-stop, who acts on your initiative and returns to normal time with you.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:fantascience]
>   [storage:item]
>   [time]
>   [self]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Timestop
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Timestop
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Timestop; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Timestop
> Range: Self
> Duration: 1+1d4 rounds
> Effect: Caster acts freely while time is stopped for all others
>
> All other creatures and objects frozen. Caster acts normally.
> Cannot directly harm frozen creatures. Time resumes at duration end.
> Source: Master Set artifact table C2 (M10); RC ninth level list.
> [Synthesis: no-harm rule extrapolated from BECMI standard.]

  <div class="power-return">

## Magic Door

> **Magic Door**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 14 **R:** near (~3 m / 10 ft)
> **T:** one wall, floor, ceiling, or ground section **D:** 7 uses or until dispelled
>
> You create an invisible personal passage through up to 10' of nonliving solid material. Only you can use the passage. Each one-way traversal consumes one use.
>
> The portal is undetectable except by detect-magic methods and is removed by dispel magic.
>
> Reverse form, Magic Lock, seals one portal-like opening beyond knock-class bypasses; only the caster can pass until uses are exhausted or dispelled.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - increase passage depth to 15'. x4 - grant one keyed ally access for the remaining uses.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [portal]
>   [access]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Magic Door
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Magic Door
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Magic Door; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Magic Door
> Range: 10'
> Duration: 7 uses
> Effect: Creates one passage
>
> Creates an invisible caster-only passage through up to 10' of nonliving material.
> Reverse form is a stronger lock that resists knock-class bypass and lasts for seven uses.

## Teleport any Object

> **Teleport any Object**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 14 **R:** touch
> **T:** one creature or nonliving object up to 500 cn per user Level **D:** instantaneous
>
> You teleport a touched target using teleport-style destination risk rules. Nonliving objects are valid targets, including detached material volumes up to one 10' cube from larger structures.
>
> If another creature holds the target object, that creature may resist with a penalized save.
>
> Special clause: when you target yourself with this power, mis-teleport error does not apply.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - expand safe transfer envelope for delicate objects. x4 - include one adjacent bound item as part of the same transfer.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [teleport]
>   [utility]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Companion Set; spell: Teleport any Object
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Teleport any Object
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Teleport any Object; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Teleport Any Object
> Range: Touch
> Duration: Instantaneous
> Effect: Causes 1 object to teleport
>
> Uses teleport error tables for touched targets, including objects.
> Caster self-teleport via this spell has no chance of error.

# Duration and Binding Rituals

Use these for long-duration effects, wards, geasa, and binding magic. Covers ritual magic, persistent enchantments, and field effects.

<div class="power-card" markdown="1">

## Dispel Magic

> **Dispel Magic**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 6 **R:** far (~35 m / 120 ft)  
> **T:** one spell effect, enchanted creature state, or magical item interface **D:** instant
>
> You apply targeted counterforce to unravel an active magical effect. Compare your user Level against the originating effect strength; equal or higher force cancels cleanly, while weaker force may only suppress or partially unwind at referee call.
>
> This can also end ongoing buffs, barriers, compulsions, and summoned bindings in range.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - target up to two separate active effects in line of sight; x4 - on successful dispel, leave a brief null-afterglow that prevents reapplication of the same effect for 1 round.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [abjuration]
>   [counterforce]
>   [utility]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: Dispel Magic
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Dispel Magic
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Dispel Magic; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Dispel Magic
> Range: 120'
> Duration: Instantaneous
> Effect: Cancels one magical effect
>
> This spell cancels magical effects, if the
> caster's level is sufficient compared to the
> original effect source.

  <div class="power-return">

## Hold Portal

> **Hold Portal**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 2 **R:** near (~3 m / 10 ft)  
> **T:** one normal door, hatch, gate, or similar closure **D:** 2d6 turns
>
> You temporarily jam a closure into its current state with low-tier arcane pressure. The target cannot be opened by normal force for the duration unless broken.
>
> This does not reinforce wall structure around the closure.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - include one additional adjacent closure; x4 - closure emits an audible warning tone to you when first forced.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]

> Range: 10'
> Duration: 2d6 turns
> Effect: Holds one door shut
>
> This spell magically holds a normal door
> closed against opening attempts for the
> duration.

## Knock

> **Knock**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 4 **R:** far (~55 m / 180 ft)  
> **T:** one locked, barred, welded, or magically sealed closure **D:** instant
>
> You emit a precision unlocking pulse that defeats mundane and many magical closure states. Doors unlatch, bars release, and lock patterns unravel long enough for immediate entry.
>
> Extremely high-tier wards may require a contested force check or partial success at referee call.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - open up to three linked closures in line of sight; x4 - also suppresses re-locking or auto-seal effects on the target for 1 turn.
>
> See also: `Knock / Lock` in the SDM Powers Index for the broadened lock-state variant.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [abjuration]
>   [utility]
>   [breach]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: Knock
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Knock
>   - file: Synthetic_Dream_Machine_04_Powers_Index.md; related: Knock / Lock
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Knock; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Knock
> Range: 180'
> Duration: Instantaneous
> Effect: Opens one locked entry
>
> This spell opens stuck, barred, locked, or
> wizard-locked doors and similar closures.

## Wizard Lock

> **Wizard Lock**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 4 **R:** touch  
> **T:** one door, gate, hatch, chest, or similar closure **D:** permanent until dispelled or released
>
> You seal a closure with keyed arcane pressure. Opening the locked target now requires either the original key-pattern, substantial forced entry, or explicit countermagic. The lock does not reinforce the object itself; it reinforces access-state and resistance to opening.
>
> Creatures of much higher Level than you may force passage with enough time and leverage, but the entry always leaves obvious disturbance.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - apply the lock to all linked closures in a small structure (up to 3); x4 - when a locked closure is forced, you immediately sense the breach if on the same map region.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [abjuration]
>   [binding]
>   [ward]
>   [imbued]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: Wizard Lock
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Wizard Lock
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Wizard Lock; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Wizard Lock
> Range: 10'
> Duration: Permanent
> Effect: One lock, or one door up to 30' x 20'
>
> This spell magically locks a door, gate,
> chest, or similar object. The target cannot
> be opened by normal means while the
> lock holds. A Knock effect or stronger
> dispelling power can release it, and very
> strong creatures may force it with effort.

## Wizardry

> **Wizardry**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 14 **R:** self  
> **T:** one magic-user-only device or one scroll spell of 1st or 2nd level **D:** 1 turn or until discharge
>
> You borrow the operating grammar of a magic-user long enough to use one arcane device or one qualifying arcane scroll effect otherwise barred to you.
>
> While the invocation lasts, you understand the item's activation pattern and are treated as the minimum caster level required to produce the borrowed effect.
>
> This does not let you cast 3rd-level-or-higher magic-user scroll spells, even if they appear on the scroll.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - keep the handling window open for the full duration even after one failed or interrupted activation attempt; x4 - while active, also read the operating cues of one additional magic-user-only item without discharging it.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [cross-tradition]
>   [item-use]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Wizardry
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Wizardry
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Wizardry; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Wizardry
> Range: 0 (cleric only)
> Duration: One turn
> Effect: Allows the use of one magic-user device
> or scroll spell
>
> Lets the caster use one magic-user-only device
> or a scroll containing a 1st or 2nd level
> magic-user spell, treating the caster as the
> minimum level needed for that effect.

  <div class="power-return">

    </a>

## Anti-Magic Shell

> **Anti-Magic Shell**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 12 **R:** self  
> **T:** self-centered personal barrier **D:** 12 turns (~2 hours)
>
> You raise a skin-tight null boundary around yourself that blocks all spell and power effects crossing the shell in either direction. Incoming powers fail at the barrier. Your own powers also cannot pass through while the shell is active.
>
> You may end the shell at will. Other than Wish-scale exception handling, ordinary countermagic cannot cancel it.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — permit one pre-declared allied support effect to pass the shell once; x4 — shell grants brief suppression pressure that forces nearby ongoing magical effects to test stability at referee call.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [abjuration]
>   [anti-magic]
>   [ward]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: Anti-Magic Shell
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Anti-Magic Shell
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Anti-Magic Shell
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Anti-Magic Shell; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Anti-Magic Shell
> Range: 0 (Caster only)
> Duration: 12 turns
> Effect: Personal barrier which blocks magic
>
> This spell creates an invisible barrier less
> than an inch from the caster's body. The
> barrier stops all spells and spell effects,
> including the caster's. The caster may end
> it at will; otherwise it lasts for duration.
> Except for Wish, no magical power
> (including Dispel Magic) cancels it.

## Barrier

> **Barrier**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 12 **R:** near (~18 m / 60 ft)  
> **T:** one cylindrical hazard field up to 30 ft diameter and 30 ft high **D:** 12 turns
>
> You establish a visible wall of whirling force-hammers that blocks passage and punishes breach attempts. Creatures that pass through take heavy impact damage with no save.
>
> The field is ideal for corridor denial, gate sealing, and forced route control.
>
> _Reverse — Remove Barrier:_ Destroy one cleric `Barrier` or one compatible wall effect (`Wall of Ice`, `Wall of Fire`, or `Wall of Stone`).
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — increase diameter and height by 50%; x4 — barrier also imposes forced pushback on creatures that fail to cross cleanly.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [barrier]
>   [control]
>   [battlefield]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Companion Set; spell: Barrier
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Barrier
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Barrier; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Barrier*
> Range: 60'
> Duration: 12 turns
> Effect: Creates whirling hammers
>
> Creates a magical barrier up to 30' wide
> and 30' high. Creatures passing through
> take 7d10 damage with no saving throw.
> Reverse form destroys one compatible
> barrier spell effect.

  <div class="power-return">

## Force Field

> **Force Field**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 16 **R:** far (~35 m / 120 ft)  
> **T:** one invisible immovable force shape up to 20 ft radius sphere or 5,000 sq ft total surface **D:** 6 turns
>
> You create a seamless barrier or object of pure force. It may take the form of a sphere, hemisphere, flat surface, cylinder, box, or part of those shapes, but it must remain perfectly smooth and regular.
>
> Nothing crosses the field by ordinary means: attacks, missiles, breath, and spells all rebound. Teleportation, Dimension Door, and planar transit can bypass it. The field cannot be broken except by Disintegrate or Wish, and even Dispel Magic cannot affect it.
>
> A sealed field preserves enclosed creatures from starvation, suffocation, and natural death while it lasts.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - refine the geometry for more exact enclosure or bridge-like support; x4 - harden one declared seam against teleport or phase bypass until the start of your next turn, unless struck by Wish-scale exception handling.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [barrier]
>   [force]
>   [ward]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Force Field
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Force Field
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Force Field; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Force Field
> Range: 120'
> Duration: 6 turns
> Effect: Creates an invisible barrier
>
> Creates an immovable force shape that cannot
> be harmed except by Disintegrate or Wish.
> Nothing passes through it normally, though
> teleportation and planar travel may bypass it.

  <div class="power-return">

## Contingency

> **Contingency**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 18 **R:** touch  
> **T:** one creature or item plus one stored non-damaging spell of 4th level or lower **D:** indefinite until triggered
>
> You bind a predeclared spell response to one specific future condition. When that exact situation next occurs, the stored spell fires immediately as though cast at that instant.
>
> The trigger may be detailed, but it must concern something within 120 ft of the triggering event. The stored spell's target and effect must be fully specified in advance. If the trigger language is incomplete or impossible to resolve, nothing happens.
>
> No creature or item can carry more than one Contingency at a time.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - harden the trigger against interruption, disguise, or split-second ambiguity; x4 - permit one tightly specified fallback target or destination if the primary resolution state is invalid when the trigger fires.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [binding]
>   [trigger]
>   [ward]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Contingency
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Contingency
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Contingency; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Contingency
> Range: Touch
> Duration: Indefinite
> Effect: Prepares one other spell
>
> Stores one non-damaging magic-user spell of
> 4th level or less behind a stated trigger.
> When that exact situation occurs, the spell
> goes off immediately. Only one contingency
> may affect any item or creature.

  <div class="power-return">

      ↩ Back
    </a>

## Protection from Lightning

> **Protection from Lightning**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 8 **R:** touch  
> **T:** one creature and carried gear **D:** 1 turn per user Level
>
> You grant electrical damage immunity up to a finite absorption budget equal to 1d6-equivalent per user Level. Deduct incoming lightning damage dice from the pool until exhausted.
>
> While active, the target is highly resistant to lightning attacks and gains strong survival margin against storm/artillery effects.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - extend protection to one adjacent ally at reduced pool size; x4 - convert excess absorbed lightning into one retaliatory discharge action.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [ward]
>   [lightning]
>   [druid]

>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Protection from Lightning

osr:
> Protection from Lightning
> Range: Touch
> Duration: 1 turn per level of the caster
> Effect: Protects against lightning attack
>
> Negates a number of lightning damage dice
> equal to caster level. Protection applies
> across multiple strikes until exhausted.

## Turn Wood

> **Turn Wood**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 12 **R:** near (~9 m / 30 ft)  
> **T:** one invisible force-wave 120 ft long and 60 ft tall **D:** 1 turn per user Level
>
> You launch a broad horizontal pressure-front that repels and captures wooden objects. The wave begins within range, immediately travels in one direction you choose at 10 ft per round, and may continue up to 360 ft total.
>
> Wooden items that touch the wave become stuck to it and move with it. Bows, spears, staves, wands, siege timber, planks, hatches, and similar objects can be displaced or rendered unusable while trapped. The wave does not harm the objects, and it does not move permanent constructions.
>
> You may stop the wave early, but once stopped it cannot move again. The stationary wave remains in place until duration ends or you dismiss it with one full round of concentration.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - spare named wooden objects or lanes from capture when placing or steering the wave; x4 - apply full displacement pressure to large wooden vehicles or siege gear not anchored as permanent structures.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [force]
>   [wood]
>   [control]
>   [druid]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Turn Wood
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Turn Wood
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Turn Wood; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Turn Wood
> Range: 30'
> Duration: One turn per level of the druid
> Effect: Pushes all wooden items away
>
> Creates an invisible wave of force 120 ft long
> and 60 ft tall that moves 10 ft per round,
> carrying contacted wooden objects with it.
> It can be stopped once, needs no concentration,
> and cannot move permanent structures.

## Immunity

> **Immunity**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 18 **R:** touch  
> **T:** one creature **D:** 1 turn per user Level
>
> You weave a broad-spectrum protective field around the recipient. For the duration, the target is completely immune to all Power Level 1–6 effects (OSR spells 1st–3rd level). Power Level 7–10 effects (4th–5th level) work at half normal potency — or at one-quarter if the recipient passes a Save vs. Spells.
>
> Any quantifiable aspect of a reduced effect — damage, duration, bonuses, penalties — is halved (or quartered on a successful save). Fractions favor the protected creature.
>
> The protection also grants complete immunity to mundane and silver projectiles and to normal weapons. Magical weapons deal half damage.
>
> The recipient may drop the protection voluntarily for 1 round by concentrating, allowing beneficial effects to function normally. The field returns automatically at the start of the next round.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — extend full immunity to Power Level 7–8 effects and halve magical weapon damage; x4 — full immunity extends to Power Level 1–10, with reduced-immunity applying to Power Level 11+ only.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:fantascience]
>   [storage:item]
>   [ward]
>   [protection]
>   [immunity]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Immunity
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Immunity
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Immunity; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Immunity
> Range: Touch
> Duration: 1 turn per level
> Effect: Immunity to 1st–3rd level spells; half from 4th–5th; full immunity
> to mundane/silver missiles and weapons; half from magical weapons.
>
> Recipient can drop protection for 1 round via concentration.
> A careful Wish can extend coverage.

## Mind Barrier

> **Mind Barrier**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 16 **R:** near (~3 m / 10 ft)  
> **T:** one creature (unwilling targets may Save vs. Spells to avoid) **D:** 1 hour per user Level
>
> You raise an impenetrable lattice around the recipient's mental presence. While the barrier holds, no form of ESP, clairvoyance, clairaudience, crystal-ball contact, or other mental surveillance or remote-influence technique can reach the target — to any such probe, the creature simply does not exist.
>
> In addition, the recipient gains +8 to all Saves against mind-influencing effects: all forms of charm, illusions, phantasms, feeblemind, and similar attacks. A natural roll of 1 always fails regardless of bonuses.
>
> _Reversible — Open Mind:_ Touch range; the target becomes fully exposed to every mind-influencing effect listed above and suffers –8 to all related Saves for the duration. Requires a successful attack roll against an unwilling target.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — the save bonus increases to +12, and one already-active dominance or charm effect is immediately suppressed; x4 — the barrier also prevents reality-manipulation attacks (geas, quest, and similar bindings) from taking hold for the duration.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:fantascience]
>   [storage:item]
>   [ward]
>   [mind]
>   [protection]
>   [reversible]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Mind Barrier
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Mind Barrier
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Mind Barrier; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Mind Barrier*
> Range: 10'
> Duration: 1 hour per level
> Effect: Protects against mental influence and surveillance
>
> Blocks ESP, clairvoyance, clairaudience, crystal ball, and other mental
> detection/influence for the target. +8 to saves vs. charm, illusion,
> feeblemind, and similar attacks. Reverse (Open Mind): touch, –8 to saves,
> unwilling target requires attack roll.

## Permanence

> **Permanence**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 16 **R:** near (~3 m / 10 ft)  
> **T:** one active MU spell effect of 7th level or less **D:** permanent until dispelled
>
> You anchor an active magical effect in place, making it permanent until a dispel magic removes it — at normal dispel chances for the caster or a higher-level spellcaster.
>
> Constraints:
> - Cannot make permanent any effect with instantaneous or already-permanent duration (fireball, lightning bolt, disintegrate, etc.)
> - Cannot affect clerical spells or 8th- or 9th-level MU spells
> - One permanence per item or area; two maximum per creature; up to five on a weapon (each permanence on a weapon beyond the first carries a 25% noncumulative failure risk — if it fails, the weapon is destroyed)
>
> The referee decides whether any given combination is eligible; spell pairings that could destabilize a campaign should be reviewed before play.
>
> Common examples: detect magic, protection from evil, read languages, fly on creatures; light, confusion, cloudkill on areas.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — the permanence can anchor a 6th-level effect even with a shorter preparation window; x4 — a permanence failure on a weapon does not destroy it, merely wastes the casting.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [binding]
>   [duration]
>   [ritual]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Permanence
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Permanence
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Permanence; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Permanence
> Range: 10'
> Duration: Permanent until dispelled
> Effect: Makes one MU spell of 7th level or less permanent
>
> Cannot affect instantaneous/permanent-duration spells, clerical spells,
> or 8th–9th MU spells. Max 1 permanence per item/area, 2 per creature,
> 5 per weapon (25% failure risk per weapon extra after first — failure
> destroys weapon). Dispelled by dispel magic at normal chances.

  <div class="power-return">
    &nbsp;&nbsp;
    <a class="js-back-link" href="#chapter-06-power-index-anchor" aria-label="Back to previous page">
      ↩ Back
    </a>

## Prismatic Wall

> **Prismatic Wall**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 18 **R:** far (~18 m / 60 ft)  
> **T:** a fixed point **D:** 6 turns
>
> You call into being a shimmering spectrum barrier at a fixed point within range. Choose one of two geometries at casting:
>
> - **Sphere:** A globe with 10-foot radius centered on the target point.
> - **Wall:** A flat vertical surface of up to 500 square feet, any shape, anchored to available structure.
>
> The wall is a multi-layered spectral barrier — each layer projects a different color with a distinct hazard for any creature passing through: fire, cold, lightning, petrification, transmutation, and so on, in sequence. Passing through all layers requires surviving each in turn. Attacks and spells that cross the barrier are absorbed or redirected depending on the layer struck.
>
> Creatures inside a sphere at the moment of casting are unaffected by it from the inside and may move freely within.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — duration extends to 12 turns and sphere radius rises to 20 feet; x4 — passing through any layer in the first 3 turns requires a Save vs. Death Ray in addition to the layer-specific effect.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:fantascience]
>   [storage:item]
>   [barrier]
>   [ward]
>   [area]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Prismatic Wall
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Prismatic Wall
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Prismatic Wall; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Prismatic Wall
> Range: 60'
> Duration: 6 turns
> Effect: 10' radius sphere or 500 sq ft wall; multi-layered spectrum barrier
>
> Source: Master Set artifact table D3 (M9); RC ninth level list.
> [Synthesis: layered effect details extrapolated from artifact table summary
> and BECMI Prismatic Wall standard — referee determines specific layer
> sequence and effects at table.]

## Symbol

> **Symbol**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 16 **R:** touch  
> **T:** one inscribed surface or a fixed mid-air point **D:** permanent (until triggered once)
>
> You inscribe a single glyph of hazardous power on any surface or in mid-air, choosing one of six types at the time of casting. The symbol cannot move; if placed on a mobile object, it remains fixed in space as the surface leaves it.
>
> **Trigger:** Any living creature that passes through, touches, or reads the rune activates it immediately with no saving throw. Exception: a magic-user (or any creature that can cast MU spells) who only reads or touches (but does not pass through) may Save vs. Spells to negate the effect for themselves.
>
> **Six symbol types:**
> - **Death** — kills any creature with 75 hp or fewer instantly.
> - **Discord** — victim attacks its nearest ally or becomes confused (as confusion) — permanent until dispelled.
> - **Fear** — victim flees at Running Speed for 30 rounds.
> - **Insanity** — victim becomes incapacitated permanently until dispelled.
> - **Sleep** — victim falls into unawakenable sleep for 1d10+10 hours or until dispelled.
> - **Stunning** — affects any creature with 150 hp or fewer; stunned for 2d6 turns.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — trigger radius extends to 10 ft, affecting all creatures within that zone when any one activates it; x4 — the symbol resets once after its first trigger, activating a total of two times before permanent discharge.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [trap]
>   [binding]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Symbol
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Symbol
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Symbol; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Symbol
> Range: Touch
> Duration: Permanent (until triggered)
> Effect: Creates one magical rune of one of six types
>
> Choose one type at casting. Triggers automatically (no save) when
> any living creature passes/touches/reads it. MU-types who only
> read/touch (not pass) may save vs. spells. Types: Death (≤75 hp),
> Discord (confusion, perm), Fear (30r), Insanity (perm), Sleep
> (1d10+10 hrs), Stunning (≤150 hp, 2d6T).

  <div class="power-return">
    &nbsp;&nbsp;
    <a class="js-back-link" href="#chapter-06-power-index-anchor" aria-label="Back to previous page">
      ↩ Back
    </a>
  </div>

</div>

## Anti-Plant Shell

> **Anti-Plant Shell**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 10 **R:** self  
> **T:** self-centered personal barrier **D:** 1 round per user Level
>
> You create an invisible skin-close barrier that blocks attacks and contact effects from plants and plant-like entities.
>
> While active, you may physically pass through dense natural growth and leave a traversable path for others. You cannot make direct physical attacks against plant targets through the barrier; spell-based interactions still function.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - brief extension to one adjacent ally inside arm's reach; x4 - barrier also suppresses one plant-entangle or vine-control effect in contact with you.

>
> You project an invisible exclusion shell that blocks attacks from normal and giant animals, insects, and other nonfantastic creatures of animal intelligence.
>
> While protected, you cannot physically attack affected creatures; both sides are mutually blocked from bodily harm through the shell unless spell-mediated.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - grant brief exclusion aura to one adjacent ally; x4 - repulse affected creatures on contact, forcing immediate retreat movement.

# Creation and Conjuration

Use these for object creation, golem manufacture, simulacra, and bringing forth. Covers summons, constructs, and materialization.

<div class="power-card" markdown="1">

## Floating Disc

> **Floating Disc**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 2 **R:** near (2 m / 6 ft from caster)  
> **T:** one hovering force-disc **D:** 6 turns (about 1 hour)
>
> You conjure a horizontal disk of force that follows you at short distance and carries gear, salvage, or fragile cargo. The disc hovers about waist-height, follows your movement path, and cannot pass through solid barriers narrower than its footprint.
>
> The disc does not grant flight; it is a load-bearing transport surface. If forced beyond carrying limits, it collapses and drops its cargo.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - increase carrying capacity by one additional burden slot; x4 - create a second linked disc that follows the first.
>
> See also: `Floating Disc` in the SDM Powers Index for the existing stylized rendition.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [conjuration]
>   [utility]
>   [movement]

>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Floating Disc
>   - file: Synthetic_Dream_Machine_04_Powers_Index.md; related: Floating Disc
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Floating Disc; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Floating Disc
> Range: 0
> Duration: 6 turns
> Effect: Disc remains near caster
>
> This spell creates an invisible horizontal
> disc that floats near the caster and carries
> equipment and treasure. It follows the
> caster's movement and remains within a
> short trailing distance until duration ends.

## Wall of Stone

> **Wall of Stone**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 10 **R:** near (~18 m / 60 ft)  
> **T:** one vertical stone wall up to 1000 cubic ft (2 ft thick) **D:** permanent until broken or dispelled
>
> You extrude shaped stone into a solid vertical barrier exactly 2 feet thick. You define the geometry freely within volume limits (for example 10 x 50 ft or 20 x 25 ft coverage), but the wall must rest on stable support and cannot appear inside occupied matter.
>
> The wall persists as real structure until physically breached or dispelled.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — increase total volume by 50%; x4 — add keyed apertures (ports, embrasures, or one controlled gate seam) during formation.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [creation]
>   [barrier]
>   [infrastructure]

osr:
> Wall of Stone
> Range: 60'
> Duration: Special
> Effect: Creates 1000 cubic feet of stone
>
> This spell creates a vertical stone wall
> exactly 2' thick. The caster chooses shape
> and dimensions up to the listed volume.
> The wall must rest on support, cannot be
> cast into occupied space, and lasts until
> dispelled or physically broken.

## Create Water

> **Create Water**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 8 **R:** near (~3 m / 10 ft)  
> **T:** one temporary spring from ground or wall **D:** 6 turns (~1 hour)
>
> You call up an enchanted spring that flows from a surface or seam for about an hour. It produces enough fresh water for roughly 12 people and their mounts for a day, with additional output at higher user Levels.
>
> This is expedition infrastructure rather than combat pressure.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — double the effective daily supply output; x4 — choose a cleaner, easier-to-store flow that immediately fills nearby vessels before the rest runs free.

>

> from the ground or wall. It flows long
> enough to create water for 12 people and
> their mounts for the day, with additional
> water at higher levels.

## Growth of Plants

> **Growth of Plants**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 8 **R:** far (~36 m / 120 ft)  
> **T:** up to 3000 square feet of normal plant life **D:** until reversed or dispelled
>
> You drive ordinary vegetation into dense overgrowth: vines, thorns, briars, and choking creepers erupt across a broad footprint. The result becomes impassable to all but giant-sized creatures and can close lanes, reshape approaches, or fortify camp boundaries.
>
> _Reverse — Shrink Plants:_ Collapse overgrowth back into a passable state or negate an earlier casting. This does not affect plant monsters.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — increase the affected area by half; x4 — the overgrowth also counts as light cover against missile fire for creatures behind it.
>
> See also: `Green Haven` for a related SDM-facing plant-shaping shelter cousin.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [creation]
>   [plants]
>   [terrain]
>   [control]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: Growth of Plants
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Growth of Plants
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Growth of Plants; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Growth of Plants*
> Range: 120'
> Duration: Special
> Effect: Enlarges 3000 square feet of plants
>
> This spell causes normal brush or woods
> to become thickly overgrown with vines,
> creepers, thorns, and briars. The affected
> area is impassable to all but giant-sized
> creatures. The reverse, Shrink Plants,
> restores passability and does not affect
> plant monsters.

## Conjure Elemental

> **Conjure Elemental**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 10 **R:** far (~70 m / 240 ft)  
> **T:** one elemental entity (typically 16 HD class) **D:** sustained while concentrating
>
> You call one elemental of a chosen type (earth, air, fire, or water) into active service. The elemental performs tasks within its capacity while you maintain control through continuous concentration.
>
> While maintaining control, your personal action economy is heavily constrained: you cannot cast other powers, cannot fight effectively, and cannot move faster than half speed. If control breaks, the elemental turns hostile and usually prioritizes the summoner.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — grant the elemental one temporary resistance keyed to its type while controlled; x4 — on release, dismiss cleanly without backlash even in unstable noosphere conditions.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [summon]
>   [elemental]
>   [control]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: Conjure Elemental
>   - becmi:Companion Set; spell-adjacent elemental interface references
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Conjure Elemental
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Conjure Elemental; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Conjure Elemental
> Range: 240'
> Duration: Concentration
> Effect: Summons one 16 HD elemental
>
> This spell summons one elemental. The
> caster must concentrate to maintain control;
> if control is lost, it cannot be regained and
> the elemental may attack the summoner.
> Controlled elementals may be dismissed by
> concentration.

## Invisible Stalker

> **Invisible Stalker**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 12 **R:** self-origin  
> **T:** one invisible stalker servitor **D:** until mission completion or destruction
>
> You summon an invisible stalker bound to complete one clearly defined mission. The servitor will pursue that task across long time and distance until complete or slain.
>
> The mission should be explicit and operationally testable (track, retrieve, guard, deliver, eliminate, or similar). Ambiguous instructions create risk of literal or hostile interpretation.
>
> `Dispel Evil` can force the stalker back to its origin plane.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — allow one contingency clause in the mission order; x4 — grant temporary noospheric trace-suppression, making the stalker harder to detect by ordinary divination.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [summon]
>   [servitor]
>   [invisible]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Expert Set; spell: Invisible Stalker
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Invisible Stalker
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Invisible Stalker; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Invisible Stalker
> Range: 0 (Caster only)
> Duration: Until mission is accomplished
> Effect: Summons one creature
>
> This spell summons an invisible stalker
> that performs one task for the caster,
> regardless of time or distance, until the
> task is complete or the creature is slain.
> Dispel Evil can force it home.

## Aerial Servant

> **Aerial Servant**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 12 **R:** near (~18 m / 60 ft)  
> **T:** one ethereal retrieval servitor **D:** 1 day per user Level
>
> You summon an intelligent ethereal servitor and assign a single retrieval mission for one creature or item at an approximate location.
>
> The servitor can carry substantial loads (up to 5,000 cn equivalent), move through many obstacles via ethereal transit, and will continue mission execution until success, timeout, or disruption.
>
> If the mission cannot be completed before duration ends, the servitor destabilizes and may return hostile toward the summoner.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — allow one fallback retrieval condition if the primary target is unavailable; x4 — grant temporary safe-return lock, preventing hostile rebound on timeout once.

## Animate Objects

> **Animate Objects**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 12 **R:** near (~18 m / 60 ft)  
> **T:** one object up to 4,000 cn or multiple smaller objects totaling that mass **D:** 6 turns
>
> You induce autonomous motion in nonliving, nonmagical objects and direct them as temporary combat or labor agents.
>
> Object behavior uses your control intent, while exact movement, defenses, and damage profile depend on size and form at referee call.
>
> Animated objects are procedural assets: statues, furniture, doors, tools, and salvage can all become short-term noospheric actuators.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — increase total animated mass by 50%; x4 — allow one animated object to continue a single predeclared task briefly without active command.

> Effect: Causes objects to move
>

> smaller ones. DM adjudicates movement,
> attacks, damage, and defenses by form.

## Clone

> **Clone**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 16 **R:** near (~3 m / 10 ft)  
> **T:** one prepared flesh sample and growth vessel **D:** permanent; growth usually 1 week per HD
>
> You grow a duplicate body from harvested living tissue. For humans and demihumans, the result is a true clone: a nonmagical duplicate that awakens as the original existed when the tissue was taken.
>
> If the original is already dead when the clone matures, the clone wakes as a restored earlier self. If both original and clone live on the same plane, a dangerous mind-link forms: shared pain, mutual awareness, and an overwhelming drive in the clone to destroy the original. Failure to resolve that conflict leads to insanity and can end in permanent, unrecoverable death.
>
> Non-humanoid results are simulacra instead: obedient enchanted duplicates with partial traits that can improve if the original is dead. Constructs and undead cannot be cloned.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - harden the growth chamber against tampering and casual detection during maturation; x4 - reinforce cross-planar separation so a matured clone kept off-plane remains link-stable until brought onto the original's plane.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [creation]
>   [body]
>   [deathless]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Clone
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Clone
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Clone; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Clone
> Range: 10'
> Duration: Permanent
> Effect: Grows one duplicate creature from a
> piece of the original creature
>
> Human and demihuman clones are exact stored
> duplicates with severe same-plane conflict if
> original and clone coexist. Other living targets
> become obedient simulacra with partial traits.

  <div class="power-return">
    &nbsp;&nbsp;
    <a class="js-back-link" href="#chapter-06-power-index-anchor" aria-label="Back to previous page">
      ↩ Back
    </a>
  </div>

</div>

## Create Normal Animals

> **Create Normal Animals**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 12 **R:** near (~9 m / 30 ft)  
> **T:** one large, three medium, or six small normal animals **D:** 10 turns
>
> You instantiate loyal normal animals at a chosen nearby point. They obey commands, can fight, carry loads, and perform practical tasks to the limit of their nature.
>
> You choose quantity class (large/medium/small), while exact species is referee-selected unless campaign doctrine says otherwise.
>
> Created animals vanish when slain or when duration ends.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 — extend command range and improve initial obedience under chaos pressure; x4 — allow mixed-size grouping within the same total output budget.

## Create Any Monster

> **Create Any Monster**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 18 **R:** far (~27 m / 90 ft)  
> **T:** created creatures totaling up to your Level in HD, or one prepared construct **D:** 3 turns; permanent for construct outcome
>
> You fabricate one or more nonhuman, nondemihuman creatures from noospheric pattern and force. Total created Hit Dice cannot exceed your Level.
>
> Creatures with three or more special abilities require prior study of a matching specimen for at least one hour. Created monsters can be blocked by Protection from Evil or Anti-Magic Shell effects.
>
> You may instead create one construct if you supply the proper materials. That construct is permanent rather than temporary, though still vulnerable to normal dispelling. Constructs with four or more special abilities usually double the already severe material cost.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - reinforce initial command stability and reduce first-round confusion in a mixed monster group; x4 - improve construct cohesion so one created construct resists the first hostile disruption check or adverse control wobble.

tags:
>   [power]
>   [type:other]
>   [storage:item]
>   [creation]
>   [monster]
>   [construct]
>   [high-tier]

meta:
> - source:
>   - becmi:Master Set; spell: Create Any Monster
>   - becmi:Rules Cyclopedia; spell: Create Any Monster
> - usage:
>   - scope: power; id: Create Any Monster; note: FTLS Chapter 06 alpha power entry.

osr:
> Create Any Monster
> Range: 90'
> Duration: 3 turns
> Effect: Creates one or more monsters
>
> Creates any nonhuman, nondemihuman monsters
> up to the caster's Level in total HD. One
> properly supplied construct may be made
> permanent, though it remains dispellable.

  <div class="power-return">

## Create Magical Monsters

> **Create Magical Monsters**
>
> _FTLS power invocation_
>
> **P:** 16 **R:** far (~18 m / 60 ft)  
> **T:** created creatures totaling up to your Level in HD, or one prepared two-asterisk construct **D:** 2 turns; permanent for construct outcome
>
> You fabricate temporary monsters with limited special abilities, choosing the creatures and bringing them into being out of thin air. Total created Hit Dice cannot exceed your Level.
>
> This version can produce monsters with up to two special abilities and may include undead, but never humans or demihumans. As with the lesser creation suite, created monsters vanish when duration ends.
>
> If you supply the proper materials, you may instead create one permanent construct with no more than two special abilities. Such constructs remain vulnerable to normal dispelling.
>
> _Overcharge:_ x2 - improve obedience and coordination across the created group's first exchange; x4 - reinforce one created construct so it ignores the first morale break, command wobble, or hostile disruption pressure it would suffer.

>
> If harmed, a summoned animal usually flees unless it arrived into an active fight on your behalf.
